Current Commentary

The Indian National Liberation Movement

— Lang

Gandhi, who had not made any political statements for more than two years, recently spoke at the village and town industry exhibition held at the All-India National Congress in Faizpur. He stated, "Please tell me the path I should follow. I am ready to return to prison and face hanging. If you can follow me, the British Governor-General of India will surely recognize his mistake and willingly return to England with other Englishmen on the next departing ship." This speech clearly indicates that Gandhi will resume political activity.

In the early stages of the Indian national independence movement, Gandhi's position was very important. However, in recent years, the leadership of the Indian independence movement has shifted to Nehru. Gandhi lost his leadership position because his political views were not supported by the majority of the Indian people. Gandhi advocated using passive methods to expel the ruling forces of the British Empire to achieve national independence. These passive methods included non-cooperation, non-resistance, civil disobedience, and refusal to pay taxes. The result of applying these passive methods for many years did not force the British government to make significant concessions. Therefore, the majority of the people demanded more aggressive and active methods. Nehru, a national socialist, is the leader of this faction. He advocates for the industrialization and modernization of India and supports the adoption of a policy of armed resistance. He strongly opposes the Indian Constitution formulated by the British government in 1935 because they demanded the complete independence of the Indian nation. Although the Indian Constitution stipulated that the Indian Federation and the governments of various provinces had some autonomy, important national powers such as national defense and diplomacy were still in the hands of the British-appointed Governor-General of India. The Governor-General had the special power to suppress any revolutionary movement at will. Therefore, at the All-India Congress in the first half of the year, Nehru said that the constitution was the shackles of slaves and must be broken. At the All-India Congress on the 28th of this month, a resolution was also unanimously passed opposing this constitution. Because Nehru's proposals have been enthusiastically supported by the majority of the people, Gandhi's past leadership has shifted to Nehru.

However, now Gandhi has suddenly broken his two-year silence and resumed political activity. What impact will this have on the future of the Indian national movement? According to reporters' observations, this is a very optimistic phenomenon. Because there are still many people in India who believe in Gandhi, and he is still working hard for the national liberation movement. Especially in recent years, due to the great development of the Indian national independence movement, Gandhi's thoughts have been greatly influenced. Not long ago, Gandhi told a reporter from the Associated Press: "India loves me and believes in me, so I feel that the mission of my life is not over yet. I still yearn for India to gain freedom and be liberated from the rule of foreigners." As long as Gandhi can accept the demands of the masses, the Nehru faction will move towards national independence under his leadership. Because the Indian people already know that to achieve the goal of complete liberation, they must establish a unified national struggle front. Dr. Anup Singh said in the conclusion of an article on the Indian national movement in the October issue of Asia Magazine: "The political atmosphere in India shows that Gandhi will soon be invited to lead the people forward again, and Nehru will be happy to accompany him." We hope that the Indian national liberation movement can embark on this unified front as soon as possible. Because only in this way can the Indian nation achieve complete liberation. This is not only true for the Indian national independence movement, but also for the national liberation movements of other countries.

Hitler Returns to Berlin to Discuss the Spanish Issue; Considers the Anglo-French Note as "Misdirected"; The German Government Will Temporarily Not Respond to It

Munich Hitler has returned to Berlin and will consult with senior Nazi Party officials on important matters. The note from the British and French governments to the German government regarding Germans serving in the Spanish Nationalist Army will naturally also be on the agenda. (Reuters dispatch on the 29th)

(Berlin) Today, officials commented on the notes sent by the British and French governments to Germany regarding non-interference in the Spanish Civil War, calling them "misdirected diplomatic documents." It is said that the German government had already made grand proposals regarding volunteer forces, but its efforts were unsuccessful due to disagreements between Soviet Russia and major factions in France. This loss is difficult to compensate for with untimely diplomatic actions. As for the questions raised in the Anglo-French notes, the German government does not seem likely to respond for the time being. Regarding the dispatch of volunteer forces, one spokesperson said that it was "not very simple." (Reuters dispatch on the 29th)

(London) The British government, together with the French government, yesterday sent notes to Germany, Italy, Portugal, and Russia, advising them not to send any more volunteer soldiers to Spain to participate in the civil war, and requesting that each country make a decision quickly. So far, none of the four governments has submitted a response. Regarding Germany's attitude, well-informed sources here recently declared that Britain does not intend to grant economic benefits to Germany as a condition for it to accept the prohibition of volunteer soldiers from serving in Spain. Germany must guarantee that it will no longer continue to build up its military before Britain can consider making economic concessions. (Havas dispatch on the 28th)

(Paris) Responsible officials recently declared that France does not intend to grant economic preferential treatment to Germany as a condition for it to accept the advice. Such preferential treatment can only be considered later when negotiations are held on the overall European situation. However, if Germany can accept the notes proposed by Britain and France, negotiations on the overall European situation will inevitably be easier. Moreover, the notes from Britain and France were sent to Germany, Italy, Portugal, and Russia at the same time, and are therefore multi-lateral in nature. Granting economic preferential treatment only to Germany would be contrary to the original intention of multi-lateral negotiations. (Havas dispatch on the 28th)

(London) Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov informed the British and French ambassadors in Moscow that the Soviet Russian government, in principle, agreed with Britain and France's proposal to prohibit foreign volunteer forces from entering Spain. (Reuters dispatch on the 29th)

The Spanish Government Releases Detained German Ship; Confiscates Cargo and Munitions; Germany Denies Sending Additional Warships

Bilbao The Basque Autonomous Region government recently issued a public announcement stating that after the German merchant ship "Palos" was detained by government warships in the waters of this region, the warship "Königsberg" sent by the German government has now arrived in this port. The captain of the ship immediately requested the autonomous region government to immediately release the ship, its crew, passengers, and all cargo on board. The autonomous region government responded that it could do so except for the munitions carried on the ship, which would still be detained. However, the captain of the ship refused to concede. As of now, the two sides are still continuing negotiations. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

Bilbao The local radio station recently broadcast a message stating that after the German merchant ship "Palos" was detained by Spanish government warships, the captain of the German warship "Königsberg" came to negotiate, and the ship has now been released under the conditions set by the Basque Autonomous Region government. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

Biarritz It was learned here today that after the Basque Autonomous Government and the commander of the German cruiser "Königsberg" negotiated by radio, the detained German ship "Palos" has been released, but the ship's cargo and munitions have been confiscated. (National News dispatch on the 29th)

(Berlin) Officials announced today that the German ship "Palos" detained by the Spanish government has been released and is returning to its home country. However, officials then retracted this announcement. (National News dispatch on the 29th)

(Berlin) Semi-official sources recently declared that after the German merchant ship "Palos" was detained in the waters of the Spanish Basque Autonomous Region, the captain of the German warship "Königsberg" went to negotiate, and the ship has been released by the Autonomous Region government. However, one Spaniard on board and part of the cargo are still being detained, so the matter has not been completely resolved. People in political circles said that the merchant ship "Palos" was detained on the high seas, and the Basque Autonomous Region authorities even sent personnel on board to arrest one Spaniard. This action is contrary to international law. The German government is currently considering "appropriate measures" to deal with the situation. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

Madrid The government today decided to release the detained German ship "Palos" and three German sailors, but the authorities in Bilbao refused to hand over the ship because it was carrying contraband. (National News dispatch on the 28th)

(Berlin) Officials have revealed that Germany hopes to resolve the detention of the "Palos" ship without resorting to force. The authorities have not dispatched additional warships to Spain, and contrary to the harsh communique issued on Saturday, there is now a tendency to downplay the case. At the same time, the Basque government issued a communique in Bayonne, the content of which contradicts the German announcement. It is claimed that the "Palos" was carrying contraband war materials. According to reports, the ship was intercepted by Spanish government warships near Bilbao on December 26. (Reuters dispatch on the 29th)

(Berlin) After the German merchant ship "Palos" was detained by government warships of the Spanish Basque Autonomous Region in the waters of the region, it was rumored that German warships "Deutschland", "Admiral Scheer", cruiser "Nürnberg", and two destroyer squadrons had been ordered to sail to Spanish territorial waters. Semi-official sources recently denied this information, saying that Germany has not dispatched any additional warships to Spain other than those already present in Spanish territorial waters. (Berlin) It was learned today from reliable sources that a 6,000-ton German cruiser was ordered today to sail to Bilbao, Spain. However, the name, current location, and mission of the ship are still unknown. The ship will likely remain stationed in Bilbao to force the Spanish government to resolve the detention of the German ship. (National News Agency dispatch on the 28th)

Madrid The local defense committee received a report stating that a German ship was seen very close to the shore in Bilbao today, but it could not be identified. (National News Agency dispatch on the 28th)

Spanish Rebels Plan Offensive Strategy; British Embassy in Madrid to Move to Valencia Tomorrow

Avila General Franco, the leader of the Nationalist government, yesterday met here with General Mola, the commander-in-chief of the Nationalist forces in the north, to discuss the war situation. The meeting lasted one hour. Afterwards, he inspected various locations on the front lines. According to general knowledge, as a result of this meeting, the Nationalist forces will launch a large-scale offensive in the near future. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

Foreign residents sheltered by the American embassy are therefore urgently seeking to obtain gas masks for self-defense. It is said that the US embassy originally stored 200 gas masks, but they cannot be found anywhere today. (National News dispatch on the 28th)

Madrid The British Chargé d'Affaires in Spain, Forbes, today warned 2,000 British citizens that the situation is becoming increasingly serious and that everyone should bring a suitcase for evacuation. Embassy staff are scheduled to withdraw to Valencia on Thursday. Most foreign residents are also preparing to evacuate. (National News dispatch on the 29th)

Madrid The British government has decided to move its embassy here to Valencia, where the Spanish government is located. The 200 British citizens residing in Madrid must now decide within 24 hours whether to leave the country. British Chargé d'Affaires Forbes convened a special meeting at the embassy to explain everything to the British citizens. The situation was very tragic. Many British citizens only acquired British nationality because they were born in Gibraltar or other nearby British territories. If they do not decide to leave the country, they will lose the protection of the embassy, ​​and their lives may be in danger. As for the British government's decision to move the embassy, ​​it is because the Spanish government has no sign of returning to Madrid, and it is difficult for Forbes to maintain close contact with more important political authorities. Furthermore, it has become increasingly difficult to provide essential daily necessities to British embassy staff and British citizens still remaining in Madrid. If the embassy moves to Valencia, this difficulty can be greatly reduced. British ships can cooperate in supplying food and other items. As for the Dao and relief work, the Spanish government has consulted with the League of Nations and dispatched experts to conduct on-site investigations. It will then consider its report and make a decision. Therefore, the Spanish government cannot begin to implement the international relief plan until it receives the experts' report. Regarding voluntary organizations that are willing to work in Spain, they will continue as usual. Forbes will come to Madrid from time to time to assist in everything. (Reuters dispatch on the 29th)

(Paris) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has recently appointed Barbier as Chargé d'Affaires in Spain and ordered him to reside in Valencia. The former Chargé d'Affaires, Neuville, will remain in Madrid to protect French citizens and handle relief matters. (Havas dispatch on the 28th)

American Aircraft Transported to Spain; State Department Issues Initial License

(Washington) It was announced here today that the State Department has approved a license for the Vimalert Company to transport munitions to Spain. This is an unprecedented event since the outbreak of the Spanish Civil War. The company has been approved to export second-hand engines and aircraft worth US$2,777,700 to Bilbao, presumably for the use of government forces. The State Department said that according to existing neutrality regulations, unless specifically prohibited by law, the government cannot refuse a merchant's request for a license, and the civil war is not within the scope of the neutrality regulations. It is said that Vimalert Company is not the only one to inquire about licensing with the State Department, but because this license will cause the State Department to feel difficult, the other inquiries have not requested it. Vimalert Company, however, insisted on the request despite the State Department's advice. The State Department has now issued two licenses, one for 18 aircraft worth $720,000, and one for 411 second-hand engines worth $2,057,000. The aircraft and engines still need to be repaired, which will take about two months. If Congress passes a ban before the shipment, the State Department can still revoke the issued license. (National News dispatch on the 28th)

(Washington) The current neutrality law's provisions on prohibiting the export of munitions only apply to external wars and not to civil wars in other countries. The US State Department recently issued an export permit in accordance with this law, allowing 18 aircraft and 411 engines to be transported to Spain and delivered to the country's Republican government. However, these aircraft and engines are all old items and will take two months to repair. From now until then, the US Congress may pass a new neutrality bill stipulating that various munitions export bans will also apply to civil wars in other countries, in which case the above-mentioned export permit may lose its validity. (Havas dispatch on the 28th)

(London) Regarding the US State Department's approval of the shipment of 18 aircraft and 411 engines to Spain, responsible officials here recently declared that the British government intends to negotiate with the US State Department and explain that Britain and France have made many efforts to maintain peace and promote the implementation of the non-intervention agreement, which should not be hindered. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

(Washington) American citizens serving in the Spanish Civil War are now in danger of losing their citizenship. Congressional leaders have sought to prohibit American citizens from participating in wars in other countries. Representative McReynolds, chairman of the House Foreign Affairs Committee, stated that he intends to ask the Department of Justice to pay attention to the prohibition in the criminal law regarding this matter. Because the law stipulates that people who participate in wars in other countries must be fined $3,000 and imprisoned for one year, according to the law, it is enough to prohibit American citizens from serving in foreign troops. Senator Borah expressed his strong support for McReynolds's intention, saying that American citizens participating in European wars would cause domestic difficulties. Therefore, he supported the revocation of citizenship. Other senators, such as Pittman, also had the same opinion. It is reported that there are currently several American famous pilots participating in the Spanish Civil War. They have organized an "American Team." (National News dispatch on the 28th)

Indian Civil Party Resolves to Oppose the New Constitution; Resolves Not to Assist Britain in Wars with Other Countries; Refuses to Participate in Coronation Celebrations

Bombay The National Congress convened a meeting in Faizpur today and passed several anti-British resolutions, deciding to begin a passive resistance movement on April 1st of next year, when the new constitution is implemented. The resolutions stipulate the following: (1) If Britain goes to war with other countries, India will never participate, nor will it donate money or send soldiers to help Britain. (2) A meeting of all National Congress members will be convened to discuss effective ways to overthrow the new constitution. (National News dispatch on the 29th)

Faizpur Today, the All-India Congress, after a lengthy debate, passed a resolution refusing the Indian Government Act of 1935 and implementing the constitution against the will of the Indian people. The resolution re-proposed a request to elect a representative assembly by adult voters in order to draft a new constitution. However, the issue of whether to assume the office of Congress members will be decided after the provincial elections. The Congress also passed a resolution prohibiting members of the Northern Conference from participating in or holding in India, and the coronation celebration of the British Emperor, and clarified that the passage of this case does not express ill will or disrespect to the British Emperor personally. The Indian Government Act of 1935 stipulates the establishment of an All-India Federal Province Autonomy and responsibilities for guarantees. In addition, there are detailed regulations on the distribution of power between the Federal Parliament and the Provincial Parliaments, the administrative relations between the Federation, the Provinces, and the Indian princes, the Federal Railway Authority, and the establishment of the Railway Court of Justice, the organization of the Federal Court, the organization of the Federal and Provincial Parliaments, and suffrage. (Reuters dispatch on the 28th)

French Budget Proposal Submitted to the Senate for Discussion; Finance Minister Attends to Explain

(Paris) The French budget year runs from January 1st to the end of each year. The budget proposal for 1937 is about to begin, and the budget proposal has been drafted by the Ministry of Finance and submitted to the Chamber of Deputies for a vote. It is now being discussed by the Senate. Today, the Senate will approve each chapter on income in the original proposal passed by the Chamber of Deputies, making only minor amendments to certain details, and it is scheduled to continue discussing the chapters on expenditure at 9:30 a.m. tomorrow. After some minor amendments, the entire proposal can be passed by a vote and then sent back to the Chamber of Deputies for review, and passed by both houses on December 31st. During the Senate debate today, Finance Minister Olivo attended to explain, stating that "the 1937 budget proposal is an honest budget proposal. Recalling the implementation of the previous budget proposal (i.e., this year's budget proposal), in order to balance revenue and expenditure, the government had to issue more than 300 substitute legal orders to increase revenue and reduce expenditure. However, since 1928, France's annual budget expenditure has always been between 45,000,000,000 and 50,000,000,000 francs. Among them, the principal and interest payments on various public debts account for 48% of the total budget expenditure, while various military expenditures account for 18% of the total expenditure. From this, it can be seen that the government has spent 66% of the national financial resources on paying for the burden of the last major war and avoiding the occurrence of future wars. As for the expenditure used for national production, it is only 16,000,000,000 francs, which has been reduced to the bare minimum. The amount of budget revenue and expenditure should be determined by the national economic life. According to the government's estimation, the French economy has a trend of recovery and prosperity, which can be seen from the recent increase in tax revenue. An examination of the income from various direct taxes in 1936 shows an increase of 22% compared to 1935. Moreover, according to recent statistics, the textile and steel industries have both seen a revival, the number of unemployed people has decreased, and the amount of exports has continued to increase. All of these are signs of economic recovery." Olivo concluded by expressing the hope that the arms race among various countries would not continue. Although various nations are currently independent of each other, they will soon recognize the necessity of economic unity due to the pressure of the situation. After Olivo finished his speech, the majority of the senators applauded and praised him. The chairman of the Finance Committee, former Finance Minister Caillaux, then gave a brief speech, outlining several financial principles, but expressing his overall support for Olivo's financial policy. ) (Havas News Agency, 28th)

(Paris) The cabinet submitted a bill to the Chamber of Deputies yesterday, requesting approval for the government to guarantee a huge loan of 2,250,000,000 francs to Poland, of which 1,405,000 francs will be used by Poland to strengthen its national defense, and another 845,000,000 francs will be used to build railways to connect Upper Silesia to the port of Gdynia. This bill was recently passed by the Chamber of Deputies with 590 votes to zero. Before the vote, most of the deputies expressed their opinions, saying that the good relations between France and Poland are a necessary condition for maintaining peace. Foreign Minister Delbos then gave a speech, saying that "the new agreement between France and Poland, which was concluded at the end of August, emphasizes that the efforts made by both parties to maintain peace can be mutually understood and used in an atmosphere of sincere cooperation." The materials needed for Poland's national defense will also be purchased from France. In short, Poland's national defense is closely related to France's national defense. (Havas News Agency, 29th)

Germany Massively Builds Warships; Naval Officers Also Greatly Increased; First Announcement in Three Years

(London) The German government has recently released a naval register, which is the first time in three years. The speed at which Germany has been building its fleet since 1934 can be clearly seen from this. The table lists a total of two 26,000-ton battleships that Germany has launched, and two 35,000-ton battleships that have already been started. A total of two 10,000-ton cruisers have been launched, and 12 have already been started. A total of 16 large destroyers have been launched, and 6 super destroyers have already been started. A total of 12 mine boats have already been started, and 36 submarines have been launched, with many more under construction. The Daily Telegraph quoted naval expert Mr. Bywater as drawing attention to the large increase in German naval officers, saying that this is the most noteworthy feature of Germany's naval expansion. In the past three years, the number of naval officer candidates and officers has increased from 187 to 1,160. This shows that the German government still intends to continue to expand its navy. Mr. Bywater also cited unofficial but reliable sources as saying that the number of lower-level German naval personnel has increased from 12,000 to 31,000 in the past three years, and is expected to increase to 40,000 next year. (Reuters, 29th)

Naval Issues; US Responds to Britain and Japan; Declares Reservation of Warships

(Washington) The British government previously notified the United States and Japan that it intends to invoke Article 21 of the London Naval Treaty, namely the escalator clause, to reserve five cruisers with a total of 21,000 tons that have reached their service age. The Japanese government subsequently notified the United States and Britain that it would invoke the escalator clause to reserve 15,000 tons of submarines that have reached their service age. (According to reports, Britain initially requested to reserve 40,000 tons of destroyers, while Japan, due to the small tonnage of destroyers that have reached their service age, requested to reserve submarines as compensation.) Regarding this matter, the US State Department will submit separate replies. Semi-official sources recently stated that the US reply to Britain will declare that it intends to reserve several cruisers, with a tonnage greater than that reserved by Britain. Its reply to Japan will declare that it also intends to reserve 15,000 tons of submarines. In addition, it will notify Britain and Japan that two US destroyer squadrons that have reached their service age will still be reserved. (Havas News Agency, 28th)

US Maritime Workers' Strike; Negotiations Deadlocked

(San Francisco) Representatives of shipping companies and maritime workers' unions met today to discuss the maritime workers' strike issue, but it has once again reached a deadlock. The reason is that the shipping companies still insist on being able to freely choose the officers of each ship regardless of union relations, while the union representatives insist on giving priority to hiring union members, which led to the breakdown of negotiations without any results. (National News Agency, 28th)

(New York) The situation of the sailors' strike here has become tense again today. Strike leaders claim that Ryan, the conservative leader of the International Seamen's Association, led the police to break up the picket lines along the coast. The International Seamen's Association opposes the strike, but Ryan denies leading the police. (National News Agency, 28th)

Britain Intensifies; Expanding Naval and Air Force Armaments; British Newspapers Discuss Pacific Situation; Advocate Guaranteeing Philippine Independence; US Reconsiders Airship Policy

(London) Britain's military reorganization plan will be intensified at the beginning of next year, with a planned expenditure of more than 100 million pounds more than this year. In terms of the navy, the government will build two battleships, five cruisers, one aircraft carrier, 18 destroyers, and six submarines, requiring an expenditure of 30 million pounds. In terms of the air force, it will build 2,000 aircraft, and separately manufacture a large number of aircraft parts for temporary storage for temporary assembly and application. In addition, it will complete the national industrial equipment to supply wartime needs. (Havas News Agency, 28th)

(London) "The Yorkshire Post," the mouthpiece of Foreign Minister Eden, recently published an article discussing the Pacific situation, stating that "Japanese Foreign Minister Arita will soon issue a declaration supporting cooperation between Japan and the United States to avoid an arms race in the Pacific. When a new Pacific peace treaty is concluded in the future, it can include guaranteeing the neutral status of the Philippines. If the Philippine Islands fall into the hands of Japan, the interests that Britain holds in the Far East will inevitably be threatened. Therefore, as far as Britain is concerned, it would be most welcome to conclude an agreement guaranteeing respect for Philippine independence." (Havas News Agency, 28th)

(Washington) After the successive misfortunes of the two major US airships, Akron and Macon, the airship business came to a standstill. Now the Navy Department is once again studying the new airship construction procedures proposed by the Bureau of Aeronautics. Rear Admiral Cooke, the director of the bureau, also requested the authorities to increase the strength of the Navy's combat aircraft, aviation personnel, and the convenience of coastal air stations in his annual report. According to Cooke, the former director, Rear Admiral King, submitted to Secretary of the Navy Swanson in May this year a procedure for continuing to build airships based on the report of the scientific committee that studied the airship problem for about a year. The scientific committee report strongly stated that although US airships have encountered two misfortunes, the US participation in the airship development plan should not be stopped because of this, and proposed a carefully considered procedure for building airships. It is heard that the above report and the Bureau of Aeronautics' recommendations are currently being considered by senior Navy commissioners, and a final decision on the US policy of rebuilding airships can be made based on this. (Reuters, 28th)

US New Deal; President Roosevelt; Intends to Make It Last for a Long Time

(Washington) Many New Deal laws are about to expire. The new Congress will convene on January 5th next year. The legislative procedures to be dealt with are very heavy. President Roosevelt has the backing of a majority of members in both houses. If he intends to retain them, he can make the various expired laws temporarily continue to be effective. However, what Roosevelt hopes for is a more permanent solution. When the various laws were passed, most of them stated that they were of a trial nature, so the deadlines set were also very short. The time has now come to select all the effective new programs and find ways to make them permanent, while letting other impractical ones expire. This is a method of reforming and consolidating the New Deal. The procedures are very complicated and difficult to carry out, and it is feared that it will take at least two years of Roosevelt's term in office. There are now two committees studying the possibility of simplifying the government's agency system and rationalizing the entire federal administration. They have already completed their work. President Roosevelt's advisors are now awaiting the reports of the above two committees to use as a basis for completely reorganizing the various parts of the government to save money and avoid the drawbacks of duplicated efforts. The temporary agencies established during Roosevelt's first term as president are as numerous as bamboo shoots after a rain. If all the plans are completed, they will all disappear. Temporary laws that have been effective will naturally become permanent, and the temporary agencies for these laws will also take a place in the existing parts of the government. The three most important of the expired laws and their expiration dates are listed below: (1) The law establishing the 200 million US dollar stabilization fund and devaluing the gold dollar (expires on January 30th); (2) The law on concluding reciprocal trade agreements (expires on June 12th); (3) The Neutrality Act (expires on May 1st). The United Kingdom is one of the most relevant countries to the expiration of the reciprocal trade agreement. According to news from London, the United States and Britain are currently engaged in negotiations to conclude a reciprocal trade agreement, and the progress is very smooth. However, due to the unexpired Ottawa Agreement, it is feared that it will take several months to complete. Even in the United States, the Senate may not agree with the government's move to make reciprocal trade agreements permanent, so the best result would be to temporarily extend them for a few years. The United States, Britain, and France have already established a monetary understanding when the franc was devalued, which shows that the US exchange stabilization fund will continue to exist on a permanent basis. People here are quite worried about the large amount of European money invested in US stocks and believe that the exchange stabilization fund is the best way to protect the domestic economy from foreign currency disturbances. As for whether the US president's power to devalue the gold dollar will still be retained, it is not yet known. Under another permanent law, it has been discovered that the Ministry of Finance has the power to set the price of gold bought and sold by the Federal Reserve Banks in gold dollars. Some critics believe that this power is sufficient to supply the exchange value of francs and pounds, and the flexibility required before gold was specified. The general opinion is that the situation will be different if the president continues to have the power to change the gold content of the gold dollar. Considering that President Roosevelt recently ordered Mr. McReynolds, the chairman of the House Foreign Affairs Committee, to read in detail the records of neutrality issues that occurred during the last major war and instructed him to pay attention to the report of Mr. Warren, the special prosecutor who managed neutrality affairs during the era of former President Wilson, it can be known that Roosevelt already has the idea of a new Neutrality Act and hopes to have it passed in the next Congress. The scope of the permanent Neutrality Act is naturally broader than the current temporary act. Due to the result of the Spanish Civil War, there are concerns about establishing additional regulations prohibiting the supply of military equipment and money to groups that are fighting against the government recognized by the public, but in the current temporary act, this kind of prohibition is impossible. The government can only use moral persuasion to prevent its citizens from supplying money, guns, and aircraft to the anti-government forces in Spain. The proposed new Neutrality Act may also include strict restrictions on the regulations for profiting during wartime. (Reuters, 28th)

Japanese-Russian Fisheries; Temporary Agreement Signed; Current Treaty Extended for One Year; Full Text of Protocol Released Yesterday

(Moscow) The Japanese-Soviet Fisheries Protocol was signed here this month by Deputy Foreign Affairs Commissioner Stomonyakov and Japanese Ambassador Shigemitsu Aoi. The fishing regulations for next year will be implemented in accordance with the provisions of the book. (TASS News Agency, 28th)

Full Text of the Protocol (Tokyo) The full text of the protocol extending the validity of the Japanese-Russian Fisheries Treaty is as follows: The fisheries treaty between the Japanese Empire and the Union of Soviet Socialist Republics signed on January 23, 1928, was extended by the protocol signed on May 25, 1936, which expires on December 31, 1936. However, because a new treaty cannot be concluded before December 31, 1936, the governments of the Japanese Empire and the Union of Soviet Socialist Republics have agreed to extend the validity of the fisheries treaty and related documents between the Japanese Empire and the Union of Soviet Socialist Republics signed on January 23, 1928, to December 31, 1937. The following persons, being duly authorized by their respective governments, have signed this Protocol as evidence.

Done in Moscow on December 28, Showa 11, that is, February 28, 1936 in the Western calendar, in duplicate. Shigemitsu Aoi, Stomonyakov. (Allied News Agency, 29th)

Amid the Silence of the Sui War, the Japanese and Puppet Troops Are Busy Transferring; Hot Troops Are Pouring Westward, Prince Te Is Forcibly Conscripting Recruits; Bandit Planes Occasionally Fly from Jiabusi to Suidong to Reconnoiter

Zhangbei Correspondence: Since the National Army recovered Damiao and Bailingmiao, the puppet bandits have almost completely perished in the mutiny and casualties. The preliminary stage has come to an end. In addition to coercing Prince Te to forcibly conscript Mongolian recruits to serve as sacrifices, a certain party is also realizing its predetermined plan, driving the hot troops to occupy Chahar North, seeking to advance westward, and opening up Chahar and Sui. In this situation, the war news on the Sui border has been extremely silent recently.

Transporting Military Equipment is Extremely Busy

As for the current situation of bandits and puppets in Chahar North, the transfer of troops and transportation of equipment is extremely busy. Regarding the transportation of military fire, a certain party is transporting a large batch of 180 tons of military fire, which will now be completely transported to Zhangbei one after another. On the 26th, more than ten heavy-duty trucks of wooden boards, six vehicles of kerosene and gasoline were transported from the pass. The gasoline stored in Zhangbei the day before has now been transported to Shangdu and Jiabusi for storage separately. Most of the gasoline for aircraft engines is stored in Jiabusi. The machinery and ammunition supplied to the bandits and puppets are transported out of Zhangbei at an average of about ten vehicles per day (from the 20th to the 26th), with the final destinations being Jiabusi, Nanhanchang, and Shangdu.

Hot River Troops Actively Move Westward

Regarding the transfer of troops, the Li Shouxin and Wang Jingxiu troops stationed in Zhangbei City, totaling more than 700 people, were all dispatched to Nanhanchang on the 24th. The Wu Guting troops from Kangbao Hot River, totaling more than 700 people, arrived in Jiabusi on the 25th, and were dispatched from the temple to the Shangdu front line to reinforce on the morning of the 26th. The Wu troops still have more than 8,000 people, stationed in Duolun, Weichang, and Dage. They have now received orders from a certain party to move west in full force within days. Zhang Haipeng's Hot River troops, numbering several thousand, are currently stationed in Guyuan. Since the 24th, Zhang has been conscripting a large number of pancakes and fried rice and other easy-to-carry foods from the people, and is also preparing to move west within days. The rumor that the hot troops are retreating eastward recently is actually inaccurate.

Prince Te Forcibly Conscripts Xilin Gol Recruits

According to a person from Jiabusi, on the morning of the 26th, three bandit planes flew west from the temple to scout around Suidong, and then flew back. Prince Te recently dispatched more than 20 of his subordinates to the various banners of the Xilin Gol League under Chahar North to forcibly recruit and train recruits. However, the general Mongols, in view of the heavy casualties of the recruits previously conscripted, regarded joining the army for training with fear and shrank back, and mostly fled into the pass. There were very few who responded to the call. In addition, the bandit army under Zhang Niwanzuo, stationed in Nanhanchang, has been almost completely depleted due to desertion. A few days ago, he personally went to Jiabusi to plot expansion with a certain special agency chief. It is estimated that the special agency chief has requested him to do so, so Zhang left Jiabusi on the 24th to reorganize his troops in Nanhanchang, and returned again on the evening of the 25th, running back and forth, and the situation was extremely rushed.

The Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee Adds; Wanping and Tianjin Administrative Districts; Commanded Nearby by the Beijing-Tianjin Municipal Governments; The Scope of the Two Administrative Districts Has Also Been Delineated

Tianjin Correspondence: The Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee has recently expanded the powers of the Tianjin and Beijing Municipal Governments. Hebei Province has added two administrative districts. The expansion of the powers of the Tianjin Municipal Government has been clearly ordered. All five agencies of the Hebei Province Maritime Public Security Bureau, Wuhe Water Public Security Bureau, Inland River Transportation Bureau, Tianjin District Administrative Commissioner, and Tianjin Security Commander are under the nearby command of the Tianjin Municipal Government. These five agencies will change their official document format from January next year and submit them to the Municipal Government. This may be due to changes in personnel, but it is an expedient measure and should not be criticized. On the 23rd of this month, the Political Affairs Committee further ordered the establishment of the Tianjin and Wanping Administrative Districts. The Wanping District consists of Daxing, Wanping, Tongxian, and Changping counties as administrative regions, with the Wanping County Magistrate serving as the Administrative Commissioner. The Tianjin District consists of Tianjin, Jinghai, Wuqing, Ninghe, and other four counties as administrative regions, with the Tianjin County Magistrate serving as the Administrative Commissioner. In addition to Chen Zhongyue, the original Tianjin County Magistrate, being appointed as the Tianjin District Commissioner, it is understood that Wang Lengzhai, a member of the Beijing Municipal Government, will be appointed as the Wanping District Commissioner and will be officially appointed soon. Because the Wanping District is close to Beijing City, it is under the nearby command of the Beijing Municipal Government. Because the Tianjin District is close to Tianjin City, it is under the nearby command of the Tianjin Municipal Government. The organization of the two public offices is the same as the Daming and Fangshan districts of Hebei Province, so no separate regulations will be drafted. However, personnel matters and the layout of the public offices also require considerable preparation. The two offices are expected to start operating in mid-January next year.

After the clear order was issued, the general public analyzed the jurisdiction of the two districts. Tongxian and Changping counties in the Wanping District are administrative regions of the "Eastern Hebei" puppet organization. Ninghe County in the Tianjin District is also under the jurisdiction of the puppet organization. The purpose of the authorities in setting up the districts can be thought of halfway through. However, the puppet organization itself felt greatly uneasy. Yin Rugeng convened a cadre meeting, and the puppet leaders from Tongxian and Tangshan attended. It is understood that the result was to quickly send representatives to visit a certain military authority in Tianjin to ask for countermeasures. On the morning of the 24th, Zhang Renli, the puppet civil affairs director of "Hebei East", secretly came to Tianjin from Tongxian and stayed in the Tokiwa Hotel in a certain concession. His whereabouts were quite secret, presumably as a representative of the puppet side.

The Provincial Government of Shanxi Orders County Magistrates to Conscientiously Handle Village System Improvement; Promulgates Important Points for Implementing the Village System Improvement Process; Village Chiefs to Be Selected and Sent for Training Starting March 1 Next Year

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Shanxi Provincial Government, in order to thoroughly improve local administration and increase political efficiency, has, in addition to organizing a Local Administrative Personnel Examination Committee to train county magistrates, district chiefs, section chiefs, and police officers, who are then assigned to serve in various counties, formulated and promulgated a General Outline for Improving the District System, a General Outline for Improving the Village System, and Rules for the Selection and Appointment of Village Chiefs and Deputies. It is learned that the Provincial Government has now stipulated six measures for training village chiefs and important points for implementing the process, and instructed all counties on the 26th to select and send village chiefs in accordance with these instructions. A total of 1,300 people will be selected from the entire province, scheduled to report to the province from February 24 to 28 next year and begin training on March 1. This is a prelude to the modernization of Shanxi's politics. The remarks of the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, the original text of the Provincial Government's instructions, and the important points for implementing the village system improvement process are explored and recorded as follows.

Remarks by the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs

According to the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Qiu, regarding the implementation policy of the village system improvement, "The village is the basic unit of administration. If village governance is well-managed, the foundation of politics can be consolidated and politics can be refreshed. Director Yan and Chairman Zhao, in view of this, have decided to improve the village system, and county magistrates, district chiefs, and village chiefs will all receive training to instill modern knowledge. Now, many county magistrates and district chiefs who have completed their training have been assigned to serve in various counties. After the village chiefs receive training in the future, everything will be renewed from top to bottom, and Shanxi's politics will have great progress. However, the selection of village chiefs is a crucial key to improving the village system. Whether the selection of village chiefs can find the right people is of great importance. In order to ensure that county and district chiefs handle this matter responsibly and properly, the provincial government has specifically stipulated that the excellence of the training results of the village chiefs selected in the future will be used as a standard for evaluating county and district chiefs and assisting personnel. In addition to this, it is also hoped that knowledgeable people in the province, counties, districts, and villages will pay attention to this, explain it to people who do not understand, and supervise any favoritism in the counties and districts without being polite. It is essential to ensure that good people are selected as village chiefs in every village. If every village can get a good village chief in the future, then the new village system will surely achieve perfect results after its implementation, so that village governance in our province will shine in the whole country."

Provincial Government Instructions

"The General Outline for Improving the Village System and the Rules for the Selection, Appointment, and Treatment of Village Chiefs and Deputies have been formulated and promulgated, and orders have been issued to the counties to study them in advance. This time, the village system improvement is a fundamental task for refreshing the politics of our province. The selection of village chiefs is an especially important key to improving the village system. The responsibility for whether the selected village chiefs are qualified rests entirely with the county magistrates and district chiefs. Whenever a policy is implemented, there is always the hope of achieving perfect results at the beginning of the launch and planning. However, due to improper handling, the opposite often happens. Examining the reasons, 40% are due to poor technical skills in the affairs, and 60% are due to irresponsibility in handling affairs. As a result, even if the current situation is not good, people not only dare not lightly make reforms, but also dare not lightly have the heart to reform. Thinking of this makes people shudder. Now, at the beginning of the improvement, how should all our county and district personnel encourage each other and strive to achieve complete success? It is now stipulated that the excellence of the training results of the village chiefs selected in the future will be used as a standard for evaluating the county and district chiefs and assisting personnel. For example, if a district selects 20 village chiefs, the total score of the 20 people at the end of the training will be averaged to calculate the district chief's score. The county magistrate will calculate the total number of people selected from the entire county, and the assisting personnel will be evaluated according to their assistance. A special assessment will be conducted at the end of the training. The trained village chiefs are scheduled to report to the province from February 24 to 28, 26th year, and begin training on March 1. It is essential to select and send them to the province on time. Do not delay the progress of the entire plan due to the delay of one county. All training and treatment measures are as follows: (1) The training period is set at three months, divided into military affairs, politics, and technical affairs training. (2) During the training period, board and lodging expenses will be provided by the province. In addition, each person will be paid six yuan per month by the original village that selected them. (3) Those who pass the training will be issued a certificate of qualification and will be appointed by the county as the village chief of the village that originally selected them. (4) During training, leave of absence or arbitrary withdrawal is not allowed unless there is an illness that has been diagnosed as true. Violators will have all expenses recovered. (5) Those who fail the training will not be allowed to be employed. The vacancy will be filled by the second-ranked village chief candidate from the original village that selected them, who will be sent to the province for supplementary training. (6) The round-trip travel expenses of the trained village chiefs to the province will be calculated according to the ticket price if they travel by train or car. If they travel by land, the price of eight corners will be issued for every 80 li of the journey, and the daily travel expense will be five corners, all of which will be paid from the county's local funds. The process and precautions for improving the village system are hereby printed and distributed along with the order. You are to comply with the order, supervise your subordinates to earnestly handle the matter on time, and be careful not to make any mistakes regarding this important political matter. This order."

Implementation Procedures

Implementation Procedures and Precautions for Improving the Village System in Various Counties of Shanxi Province, from January 1 to February 10, 26th year: (January 1) In accordance with the received order and instructions regarding the General Outline for Improving the Village System and the Implementation Procedures, as well as the Rules for the Selection, Appointment, and Treatment of Village Chiefs and Deputies, the following matters should be handled: (1) Report the date of the received order by telegram. (2) Notify the district chiefs and one assistant in each district to bring the latest household registration book of the district to the county for a meeting on January 3. (3) Instruct the chief of the First Section to print and prepare for distribution the key points regarding the expansion of the new village establishment and the selection and training of village chiefs, as well as the Rules for the Selection, Appointment, and Treatment of Village Chiefs and Deputies, within the General Outline for Improving the Village System and the Implementation Procedures, according to the total number of village chiefs and deputies and county and district personnel in the entire county. (4) Notify the chief of the Public Security Bureau and the chiefs of all sections and supervisors to participate in the meeting when the district chiefs and assistants are convened. (January 2) Convene the chiefs of all sections, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, and the chief of the First District to thoroughly study and understand the General Outline and Implementation Procedures, as well as the Rules for the Selection, Appointment, and Treatment of Village Chiefs and Deputies, and formulate a specific plan from the beginning to the end according to the situation in the county. Proceed in order and ensure that the plan is completed on time. Be considerate and ensure that no mistakes occur in the middle. (January 3) When all the district chiefs and assistants arrive, hold a meeting immediately. Assistants will attend to provide consultation. (1) The county magistrate will report the purpose of the meeting. (2) Discuss each article of the General Outline for Improving the Village System, the Implementation Procedures, and the Rules for the Selection, Appointment, and Treatment of Village Chiefs and Deputies clearly, and ask if there are any difficulties. After the district chiefs express their opinions as much as possible regarding the situation of the villages under their jurisdiction, study and handle the methods in detail. (3) The county magistrate should refer to the overall map of the county, the total number of households and their locations in each village, and the provisions of Articles 4 and 5 of the General Outline, and consider the actual situation. The section chiefs and district chiefs should make preliminary plans for the districts in order of resolution. The following items should be noted: A. The county magistrate should adopt the opinions of the district chiefs in the district as much as possible. The section chiefs, bureau chiefs, supervisors, etc., who know the details of the village conditions, history, mountains, and terrain, must describe them in detail for selection. B. The village establishment affairs must take into account the terrain, distance, and history of each village in the entire county, but do not temporarily accommodate the village conditions, which may cause the distance between the united villages to be too far, making it difficult to unite and causing long-term inconvenience in handling affairs. C. When making preliminary village establishments, the location of the village office should be tentatively determined for each village establishment. If the location is an independently established village, it will occupy its original village office. If it is a joint village establishment, it should be located in the village with the largest population in the village establishment. (To be continued)

Artificial Propagation of Laver; Successful Results of Zhejiang Aquatic Products Experiment Field

Dinghai Correspondence: Among the important edible algae, laver is the most delicious and valuable. It is produced along the coast and on the islands of Zhejiang Province. Statistics show that the annual output is only three to four thousand catties. Because it has always been known only to collect natural products, the output is very small and the price is extremely high. The experiment field wanted to use science to increase production. Last year, artificial propagation experiments were conducted in the waters off Putuo. Initially, due to inadequate equipment, the results were not significant. Therefore, the field director Chen Tongbai and technician Chen Chunshou re-planned in detail, and put the attached materials into the water to make them occur artificially. Recently, it has been found that the propagation is flourishing and spectacular, and the quality is better than that of natural products, and the flavor is exceptionally delicious. According to the person in charge of the field, this artificial propagation method has been completely successful. Once a way is found to make it economically viable, it will be promoted, and it will be possible to produce it in large quantities in the future to help the people's food and enrich their lives.

Jiading; West Township Captures Bandit Ship

On the evening of the 26th, a bandit ship with more than a dozen bandits arrived in Hengjing Village, Wangxian Township, Fourth District. The villagers caught sight of it, but remained calm and reported to the Waigang District Office. District Chief Xu and Inspector Zhu of the District Office and the Public Security Sub-station led dozens of militiamen and police officers to ambush and capture the ship. One bandit, Lu Ayin, from Loutang County, was captured. On the ship were two sacks of Hui's Ruizhi Yizhuang, a package of red dates, and four pawn tickets. The people and the spoils were taken to the district and then to the county for investigation.

Wuxi; Bizarre Male Corpse Discovered

A nameless male corpse was suddenly discovered yesterday in the culvert next to the field bank of a certain family in Caowangjing, Third District. The corpse was wearing a blue cloth cotton jacket and cotton pants, with a new hemp rope tied around his waist. There was an old hemp car bag next to the corpse. However, his head and upper body were drilled into the hole, and his face was unrecognizable. His waist was bent and his back was hunched, and his condition was miserable. The cause of death was bizarre.

The incident was detected by the detective team of the Public Security Bureau of this county. They ordered detective Bu Xiang to cooperate with the local water and land police corps to search and arrest them. Eleven bandit ships were intercepted on the spot, and eight bandits were arrested. A large number of stolen goods were also found on the ships. They were escorted to the city yesterday and sent to the Public Security Bureau for verification.

The police district system in Jiangsu Province has been implemented with good results. The provincial government has already promulgated the outline of the implementation measures of the police district system. According to the person in charge of the Department of Civil Affairs, the number of students recommended and applying to the police school in various counties of Jiangsu Province is very common. The police officers trained by the school were originally the cadres for implementing the police district system. Now that the experiment has been effective and beneficial to the local administration, it should be actively promoted. As for whether all counties should implement it uniformly, it depends on the efforts of local officials.

Promoting Rural Sideline Occupations

The Jiangsu Provincial Government, in view of the abnormal depression of the rural economy in various counties in Jiangbei in recent years, believes that relying solely on primary industry production is not enough to maintain the lives of farmers. Therefore, it has repeatedly ordered various counties to actively promote rural sideline occupations in Jiangbei, so that farmers can use their spare time and land with a small amount of capital to engage in production. Since the provincial government has strictly supervised the promotion in various counties, the results have been quite significant. The price of the increased products in various counties is said to have reached more than one million yuan, and the authorities are still trying to promote it.

Random Notes on a Trip to Europe (4)

— Our Correspondent in Europe, Lieshan

From then on, not only would it be impossible for Germans and Jews to marry in Germany, but even their love affairs would be subject to legal sanctions. In addition to being recognized as "racially demeaning," the two parties would also face two or three years in prison. Such cases can almost always be found in German newspapers several times a month.

Why are the National Socialists so determined to exclude Jews? We can understand that people of Jewish descent are not allowed to hold public office in Germany. But why should even private love affairs be interfered with? Some people say that Mr. Hitler was once stimulated by Jews in Vienna. Although this cannot be considered the main reason, Jews have never been welcomed by the general public in Germany, not only in Germany but also in other countries in Europe.

The discrimination against Jews in Germany is, first, because they are a different race. Secondly, Jews are good at doing business. It is very common for a grandfather to be a cattle and sheep broker, the father to be a shop owner, and the son to be a businessman or a large industrialist. (We only need to remember the life of Shanghai Jewish tycoon Hardoon.) This naturally arouses the resentment of the Germans, especially after the European War, when groups of Jews from Poland, Russia, and other places immigrated to Germany. They not only made high-interest loans to German farmers, but also took advantage of the devaluation of the German mark to speculate as much as possible. After a considerable period of time, the originally ragged brokers became wealthy households. The root cause of the Jews' resentment lies in this point. As a result, Hitler called out and everyone responded, creating the current situation. Many Germans know that this anti-Jewish policy is too inhumane, but who dares to have another opinion in the current atmosphere?

I remember once talking to a certain gentleman in charge of Jewish affairs in the National Socialist Party about this issue. He asked, "Are there any Jews in China?" I said, "Although there are some Jews in China, they have not yet become a problem. Precisely because of this, it is not easy for us to understand your country's anti-Jewish policy. If we can explain to our readers, 'Jews are like our neighbors,' then everyone will immediately understand what is going on. But Jews are a nation without a country, and why are all Jews 'inferior'?"

He said, "Jews are at home everywhere and have no concept of a country. Today they can be Germans, and tomorrow they can become French or British, as long as it is beneficial to them personally..." We often hear his theory, but all Jews are bad guys without exception. As long as a person has some Jewish blood in his body, whether on the father's side or the mother's side, or even the father's parents, a Jewish person will be classified as an "inferior race." This logic does not seem to be something we can understand. The prerequisite for a German citizen today is that he must have clean ancestors, both on the paternal and maternal sides, tracing back to 1800, when there was no Jewish blood mixed in.

Thirteen. Further Discussion on the Jewish Question

After Hitler came to power and implemented the anti-Jewish policy, people generally worried about Hitler. The reason is that almost all the financial institutions and international trade in the world are in the hands of Jews. If Jews in various countries unite to impose economic sanctions on Germany, then Germany's finances will immediately fall into a predicament. Although, as the reporter knows, Germany's foreign trade has been affected by the anti-Jewish policy in recent years, the racial consciousness of the Jews is far different from what we expected.

For example, in trade with Germany, many foreign Jewish merchants, especially Jewish merchants in Britain and the Czech Republic, have always been good customers of the industrial products of the Third Reich in recent years. They even come to Germany to purchase goods in person. Where personal interests lie, racial issues can be put aside. This is a typical Jewish merchant. On the other hand, the reason why Jews in various countries dare not actively assist German Jews is probably to expand the "anti-Jewish issue," which would affect their own status. In the eyes of Jews, it is easy to deal with the anti-Jewish issue in a single Germany. If the Jewish issue also occurs in Britain, the United States, and France, then their future will be unimaginable.

Almost everyone in every country has a sense of aversion to Jews. I remember when I was in school, if a classmate was called a "Jew," he would feel more uncomfortable than if he was scolded with other words. In European countries, an ordinary Jew cannot enjoy equal treatment unless he has special talents or money. The atmosphere of anti-Jewish sentiment, from Nuremberg (the place where anti-Jewish sentiment is the most severe in Germany) to Palestine, there are seeds of anti-Jewish sentiment wherever Jews exist.

The ideal way to solve the Jewish question may be to let them form their own country. In this way, many disputes can be avoided. Secondly, the Jews themselves should change their way of life and stop only focusing on money, which would arouse the resentment of the people of the local country. Although not all Jews are capitalists, most of the world's wealthy people are Jews, especially in many large and small cities, where the bigwigs who control economic power are also Jews. Some people say that as long as Jews engage in less industry and commerce, half of the Jewish question can be solved.

Since Germany had an anti-Jewish issue, some Jews have immigrated to South America, Palestine, Soviet Russia, and other places. I heard that some of them have also come to China. We Chinese people certainly do not talk about racial issues, but I hope that these people will not forget the reasons why they could not stand in Germany, even though they were implicated by some of their fellow citizens.

Gaoyou; Citywide Rickshaw Strike

The First Branch of the Public Security Bureau of this county, in view of the many dangers of rickshaws carrying goods and the damage to the road surface, summoned rickshaw merchants to specially manufacture 30 freight vehicles. Since the implementation, those who use rickshaws to transport goods have been detained. All rickshaw drivers believe that they can only carry passengers, and their business is very small, which greatly affects their livelihoods. Therefore, they collectively agreed to strike, so rickshaws have disappeared on the streets, and they plan to petition the county government to maintain their livelihoods.

Nanjing; Students from Zhongda University Visit Quan Hua

The College of Agriculture of the National Central University in the capital believes that in addition to chemical industry experiments, they must also visit the site to learn from it, so as to prove the gains and losses in theory. However, there are not many emerging chemical industries in Nanjing. Only the Quanhua Soy Sauce Factory outside Hsimen's Erdaogengzi can be used for research. Therefore, Professor Shen Xueyuan of the school obtained the consent of the factory in advance, and led the whole class of students to visit the factory at 2 pm yesterday. They made detailed inquiries about the manufacturing process of soy sauce, and visited the manufacturing rooms for boiling beans, making koji, squeezing oil, disinfecting, and bottling. As a result, the teachers and students were very satisfied. They believed that it was the most perfect soy sauce factory among the emerging industries in the country. Not only has it significantly improved the people's food hygiene, but it can also resist the import of foreign soy sauce and recover the rights and interests. The visit ended and they returned to school at 6 pm.

Ningbo; Prison Break Tragedy

The Ninghai County Prison holds more than a hundred thieves and other criminals. Each is nailed with shackles, and the security is very strict. Around 1 a.m. on the 27th, the criminals suddenly broke out of prison at the same time. One group broke out of the back wall, and the other group broke through the prison door, then jumped down from the roof. The shackles they were wearing were secretly filed off in advance. At that time, it was a clear moonlit night. When County Magistrate Li Hanfu heard the news, he got up in his underwear, took a gun and led the police to surround and arrest them, and ordered emergency measures to be taken and opened fire to suppress them. Sixteen escaped prisoners were shot dead on the spot and fell near the road. The situation was terrible.

Wuchang Road Opens to Traffic on New Year's Day

The Wuwei Road from Wuxiangqi in Yinxian County to Changtiaozui in Zhenhai, which is more than 30 kilometers long, was built by the Defense Command and has been completed. It is leased to Ningchuan Long-distance Bus Company for traffic. There are five stations on the entire road, and it is scheduled to open to traffic on New Year's Day.

Xiqing Basketball: Qingguang Threatens Jinan, Jinan Wins in Overtime

The Xiqing basketball team's makeup game against Chizhi at Nanyang the night before was declared forfeited due to Nanyang's absence. Last night, after Mr. Jin Guoquan, Nanyang's instructor, explained that they had not received the makeup game notification, Xiqing understood. Therefore, the Nanyang vs. Chizhi game will be rescheduled. Last night, Nanyang played against Fudan. Although Nanyang fought hard, the difference in strength was too great, and the entire game was one-sided. As a result, Fudan took a 25-11 lead, and then won again 33-16. The final score was 58-25, a big win for Fudan. The second game was Jinan against Qingguang. Jinan, confident of victory, was inevitably complacent, and did not field star players like Yin Guiren and Wang Nanzhen. Unexpectedly, Qingguang was still strong. Having posed a great threat to Xintong the night before, they put all their effort into the game last night. As a result, the Jinan team, known as a formidable force, was greatly troubled. In the first half, Qingguang led by two points with a score of 17-15. In the second half, Qingguang led twice again. Jinan caught up to 26-25, 28-25, and 30-27. Qingguang's Lu Dazhen was ejected for four fouls, but there was no replacement. With six minutes remaining, Qingguang played with four players. Ultimately, due to being outnumbered, with only one minute and forty seconds left in the game, Han Zhenyuan was also ejected for four fouls. Regrettably, Liang Guoyang, overexcited, missed the free throw at this valuable opportunity. Consequently, Cai Yanxiong tied the score at 37-37, and the buzzer sounded. After a five-minute overtime, although Qingguang only had four players, they had as many as eight shooting opportunities. Unfortunately, they missed each one by a hair's breadth, gaining nothing. Meanwhile, Jinan's Kuang Yao Ya imitated the old trick of Lan Yin, lurking under the basket. Cai Yanxiong passed from afar, and he tipped the ball in. Within two minutes, in a flash, they increased by six points. Qingguang suffered a disastrous defeat with a score of 37-49.

Educational News

National Basic Education in Guangxi in the Last Five Years: Provincial and County Funding Has Increased Annually

In Guangxi, primary schools have been renamed National Basic Education, which has two important missions. One is the transformation of education itself, making it popular and productive to achieve national revival as the ultimate goal. The other is the transformation of education for society, using education as a tool to complete the tasks of Guangxi's new politics, new economy, new culture, and new society. To actively promote this, a six-year popularization plan was formulated. On the one hand, enrollment was encouraged, and on the other hand, a compulsory education order was promulgated on New Year's Day of the 25th year. The province was divided into eight guidance areas for the popularization of national basic education, each with a guidance committee responsible for guidance and design. Each county was required to establish a central national basic school in each township (or town) and a national basic school in each village (or street). The basic political organization of Guangxi is that the provincial government is divided into eight administrative supervision areas, each governing more than ten counties. Counties are divided into districts, townships (towns in cities), villages (streets in cities), and jia. Ten households form one jia, eight to fifteen jia form one village (street), and eight to fifteen villages form one township (town). The plan aims to universally establish national basic schools in all villages (streets) of the province before July of the 25th year, universally establish central national basic schools in all townships (towns) of the province before July of the 26th year, complete short-term national basic education with a one-year period before July of the 27th year, complete national basic education with a two-year period before July of the 28th year, and complete the preliminary construction work of villages (streets) and townships (towns) throughout the province before July of the 29th year. Among the more than 25,000 villages in Guangxi, according to statistics from July of the 24th year, more than 18,000 national basic schools had been established. The funding is coordinated and allocated by various counties. Generally, the entire funding for central basic schools in townships (towns) comes from county funds, the salaries of teachers and staff in village (street) basic schools are paid by the county, and other expenses are raised by the villages and streets themselves. Since the province implemented universal education, funding has increased annually. The comparison of provincial and county national basic education funding in the most recent five years is as follows:

Based on the above comparison, the 24th year saw the largest increase in funding, with a combined increase of 807,735 yuan from the province and counties.
