Shen Bao National Goods Special Issue

A Review of the "National Goods Year for Citizens"

— Xuan Wan

In the rapidly passing flow of time, our "National Goods Year for Citizens" has quickly come to an end.

Now that the end of the year is approaching, we should also review and settle accounts for this year's national goods movement. We know that review is very important, as it can point out past shortcomings, and also show past strengths, so that we can re-determine future plans and continue to move forward.

This year's national goods movement has obviously been carried out through very arduous struggles, because of the continuous efforts of our many entrepreneurs and those who are enthusiastically engaged in the national goods movement, which has ultimately enabled the entire development of national goods to make considerable progress, especially the slight increase in exports, the reduction of import surpluses, the increase in the total turnover of general manufacturers, and the improvement in foreign trade. This gratifying trend has now been proven by facts.

As for the concrete facts - in this year's progress of our national goods, we can first mention the organization of the Nanyang inspection delegation this summer, which went to various parts of Nanyang for on-the-spot inspections, publicity, and promotion. It has opened up a considerable foundation for domestic products in overseas markets, such as the holding of family visits, which indicates that the promotion of national goods is becoming more practical and active. What is most worth mentioning is of course the preparation of the National National Goods Joint-Venture Company. The establishment of this nationwide planned and organized production and sales organization not only shows the enterprising spirit of our national goods industry and the government's determination to maintain domestic production, but also reflects our promising and hopeful national goods future.

Although there were still many obstacles to the national goods movement this year, the biggest ones were rampant smuggling and the continued fierce dumping of foreign goods. We still need to make greater efforts, especially to reduce the import of a large number of imported luxury goods, which is what we should do immediately.

The "National Goods Year for Citizens" has only a few days left. I dare to make a final five-minute appeal, wishing everyone not only to have the passion of nostalgia, bitterness, and roar for this year, but also to work hard for the promising next year as soon as possible!

A word of contribution

The Prevalence of the Use of National Goods

— Yang An

Recently, the Shanghai National Goods Movement Federation commissioned Ms. Lu Lihua to investigate and promote the national goods movement in the four provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan. Ms. Lu spent more than twenty days traveling to important cities in the four provinces, and contacted local party and government agencies and local women's circles. She received enthusiastic support from comrades in various places, who organized associations to use national goods or advocated national goods movements. According to Ms. Lu's observation, the national goods movement in various places can be said to be universally developed, and the leaders are also working tirelessly. However, there are regrets:

(1) The authorities have failed to provide full support.

(2) Financial difficulties make it difficult to implement established plans.

(3) Some of the work is not practical.

(4) The national goods movements in various places have different organizations and confusing names, and cannot be linked together to carry out expanded movement work.

Based on Ms. Lu's impressions, she believes that the promotion of national goods should have four steps.

(1) Investigate the local production and consumption of national goods.

(2) Promote the practical improvement of national goods products.

(3) Enable people to develop the ability to distinguish between national goods and non-national goods.

(4) Universally promote national goods. At the same time, the names and organizations should be unified, and a supreme agency should be established nationwide to oversee its success. Branch associations should be established at the provincial, city, county, and township levels, so that the system is clear, the organization is unified, and the power is consistent, so that the effect of fingers and arms can be achieved. Annual activity plans should be established and implemented step by step.

The prevalence of the use of national goods in various places is a very good sign for the 25th year of the Republic of China. At the end of this year, it is especially gratifying. The reporter believes that the future development and progress of national goods are unlimited. The other day, Mr. Li Zuyu showed me his translated article on the progress of the national goods movement in Japan. We feel that the situation in the Eastern neighbor more than ten years ago is exactly the same as the situation in our country today. With the full support of the government, the unanimous use of national goods by the people, the seriousness of the inspection work, the efforts of technical personnel, and the mutual encouragement of all parties in society, they have achieved today's self-sufficiency and no need to seek external help. Today, our country is united from top to bottom, with the goal of restoring rights and interests through the use of national goods. In less than ten years, the results will be considerable. What Ms. Lu has stated can be gradually realized. At the end of the year, I will briefly describe the general situation and express my infinite hope.

Farewell! "National Goods Year for Citizens"

— Zhang Mengzhao

Time flies! The National Goods Year for Citizens has only two days left! The author once wrote words to welcome its arrival, and now that it is leaving, I cannot help but feel attached! In fact, for many of the same items, it is just a psychological effect to like foreign goods; national goods are much better! Then why wouldn't I buy them!

National goods emphasize practicality, while foreign goods emphasize appearance. For things that we eat and use ourselves, we don't seek appearance, but only practicality.

It is the duty of every citizen to strive to buy national goods.

Promoting national goods should be done by setting an example and promoting it from oneself to others; if I buy national goods, others will also follow me to buy national goods, and national goods will naturally become popular!

Carrying national goods home, men, women, old and young, whether they eat, use, wear, or dress, are all national goods. It is really a house full of national goods, and the joy is harmonious

An Easy Way to Encourage the Use of National Goods

— Baling

When it comes to the issue of promoting national goods, on the one hand, it is of course hoped that the general national goods factories will make appropriate improvements in the quality of goods so as to achieve sturdiness, durability, and beauty. At the same time, it is necessary to persuade the compatriots who usually love to use foreign goods to reverse their past habits, change their ideas, and stand on the same front to work together for national goods. Only by advancing in both ways can we achieve the great effect of promoting national goods, which is a truth that no one can deny.

Regarding the first problem, I believe that the general national goods factories are already starting to work on it, which is naturally a gratifying phenomenon, so there is no need to talk much about it here. As for persuading the general public who usually love to use foreign goods to reverse their past habits, divorce foreign goods, and fall in love with national goods, this is a problem worth discussing.

The reporter recently visited Mr. Chen Diexian, an old senior in the national goods industry, Tianxu Wosheng, and talked with him about the issue of encouraging the use of national goods. Mr. Chen proposed a very good method, which I think is of great value for public introduction and public publication.

Mr. Chen said: "I receive an average of more than ten letters from people every day. Some want me to guide them in making a living, some want me to guide them in studying small industries, and some want me to guide them in academic studies. I always try my best to tell each comrade who writes to me what I know, hoping that he can find a way. However, many letters often use foreign envelopes and foreign stationery, which I think is very necessary to persuade them. Therefore, I specially engraved a seal with the six characters 'I Advise You Not to Use Foreign Goods' on it. When I encounter this kind of letter, in addition to answering the letter, I also put a seal on the end of the letter to express my meaning of persuasion. Since this method was implemented, I have rarely received this kind of letter! Perhaps this is the result of my persuasion..." After listening to the old man's words, I felt that there was a great truth in it. At the same time, I thought: We can also learn from this easy way to encourage the use of national goods. I hope that all readers will pay attention to it. If we receive this kind of letter in the future, why don't we also imitate Mr. Chen's method?

Don't underestimate this small seal of "I Advise You Not to Use Foreign Goods." You must know that this has a very important relationship with the psychological construction of the general public to promote national goods!

Re-discussing College Students and Domestic Goods

— Quan Jia

In previous issues of this magazine, there seemed to have been an article about college students using domestic goods. The author poignantly pointed out that current college students are only indulging in material civilization and are actually promoting foreign goods. However, this may only occasionally happen in universities near big cities. Most universities, such as Peking University, Zhejiang University, Central University, and Jinling University, still live frugal lives. The author himself, as well as many friends studying at universities near and far, almost all feel that university life is not as extravagant as they imagined during middle school. Especially in the inland areas, we often find four or five comrades renting a small back room together, making their own tea, mending their own clothes, and even taking on odd jobs to support themselves when they are free. This cannot be considered an encouraging reality.

However, college students are almost people who have a significant impact in the education field. Promoting domestic goods has a great relationship, both indirectly and directly. Now, let's discuss it from two aspects.

(1) Indirect aspect: College students should have the desire to contribute to the domestic goods industry. When a person is studying, the foundation for their lifelong work is almost laid. What is our lifelong work? Naturally, this is based on personal interests and should not be forced. However, as far as possible, special attention should be paid to subjects related to domestic goods. For example, those studying commerce should pay special attention to the annual statistics of foreign goods exports and the financial management of new industries. Those studying engineering should study enthusiastically the improvement of domestic goods factory equipment and the facilities of foreign factories. This may be of great help for future work.

(2) Direct aspect: First, practicing the use of domestic goods must start with oneself. It is unforgivable to buy a foreign product when one knows that a domestic product is available. Many people in society are dissatisfied with college students' empty slogans. In fact, sometimes these contradictory things do happen, which is very shameful. Second, we must awaken the general public with lagging culture to use domestic goods. The youth in the north have done a lot of practical work in the past six months, and promoting domestic goods is one of them. It is said that the results are very good. This magazine often publishes articles on how to promote domestic goods, and many of them are very practical. If you want to do it, then do it immediately and don't wait for tomorrow.

Why are college students suspected of being promoters of foreign goods? Why are they ridiculed that one more college student means one more leak for the country? Of course, there are many rich young masters in universities who wear the most fashionable clothes every day as if they are competing with each other. Of course, there are also those who are intoxicated with material enjoyment and encounter romantic lives. However, do not ignore the vast majority of progressive college students, they love to use the products of national industries, they are absolutely unwilling to follow the crowd!

We want to go further, unite the majority of comrades, and move forward with big strides towards the most beneficial path for domestic goods!

If it is allowed to flow continuously, it will eventually run out, and one day, "Alas, alas!"

As for "smuggled goods"? This is the most serious and unfortunate thing that has happened in this "Citizens' Domestic Goods Year"! It can also be said that this year's "Citizens' Domestic Goods Year" has revealed something even more terrifying than "foreign goods"! Because, on the one hand, it can reduce a country's tax revenue, or even completely cut it off! On the other hand, it can destroy a country's "domestic goods," or even completely eliminate them! Therefore, it can make a country's economy collapse faster! It is even more unimaginable!

Alas! From this point of view, both "foreign goods" and "smuggled goods" are enough to ruin our country and are the only great enemies destroying our country's economy! We must not ignore them. The Raw Material Problem of Vegetable Oil

— Sun Linchang

Since ancient times, our country has used vegetable oils, such as soybean oil and rapeseed oil, for lighting lamps. Later, since the import of cheap petroleum from foreign countries and its dumping, the people only sought immediate enjoyment and disregarded future suffering, causing the native oil plants of our country to be gradually reduced in planting, and the import of petroleum also increased year by year. Just calculating the more than five million households in Zhejiang, each household uses an average of one box of petroleum per year, and the money overflowing from the province is more than 20 million yuan. Therefore, this is also one of the reasons for the collapse of the rural economy. Now, fortunately, someone has invented a vegetable oil lamp using electrical pressure, and the "China Vegetable Oil Factory" has also emerged. The factory is jointly organized by the construction departments of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Zhejiang provinces. It is currently preparing everything and will be formally established before vegetable oil products are launched on the market this year. But I believe that after this vegetable oil lamp is promoted in the future, the production of vegetable oil will not be able to meet the demand, and the price of oil will inevitably rise, making it still difficult to compete with petroleum. Therefore, the first step for the vegetable oil factory now should be to advise farmers to plant more oil plants, such as Chinese tallow trees, camellias, rapeseed, peanuts, etc. Among them, the easiest to sow and the most effective is rapeseed. (Also known as kale mustard, commonly known as rapeseed, its seeds are used to extract rapeseed oil). Because rapeseed is planted in winter, it does not interfere with rice cultivation, and the harvest is very abundant. According to usual, each mu of field can harvest 100 jin of seeds. This 100 jin of rapeseed can extract 30 jin of oil. Each farming family can plant one mu of rapeseed, which is enough to supply the needs of the whole year. This matter is related to the national economy and the people's livelihood. I deeply hope that those in power can raise their voices, so that all mountains will respond, and it is also one of the gains of tightening the national economy and blocking leaks.

Grain: Bulls in Futures Wheat Slightly Sold Off, Market Price Fell Back with Foreign Wheat

Yesterday's market for futures wheat was generally calm in the morning session. Because the price of foreign wheat was good by 6-7 jiao the previous day, but yesterday Chicago fell by 1.4 yuan in the near term and 3-4 jiao in the long term, and Canada fell by 2 jiao, the market price stabilized after the opening, and there were few transactions. Because the flour market has stopped and accounts will be closed at the end of the year, there was little competition. Until the afternoon session, it was still stable at first. Then, non-industry bulls sold off in all months, and the market sentiment turned soft, falling back by 1-2-3 fen. The current wheat market has seen very clear deliveries in recent days. Extra-high-quality goods have been priced at more than 6.7 yuan and half a jiao, and second-quality goods at 6 yuan, 6 jiao, and 7 fen, with only a few hundred packages traded.

The Miscellaneous Grain Exchange will hold auctions for all months until yesterday, and will normally hold auctions on January 5 next year.

Flour Delivery Only 2,000 Packages

Flour Delivery Also Rescheduled to Open on the 5th of Next Year

The flour delivery for December was still lonely. Only 2,000 packages of Yuanshan Deer from the Wuxi Jiufeng Factory were delivered, and were received by this street. Otherwise, there was nothing. The market for the exchange was originally scheduled to open on January 4 of next year, and the market had been announced earlier. It is now heard that the miscellaneous grains are scheduled to be auctioned on the 5th, so it must also be delayed by one day, and it is also scheduled to be auctioned as usual on the 5th.

Early Sen Rice Traded 13,000 Packages, Thin Rice and White Japonica Continued to Rise by 1-2 Jiao

(Early Sen Rice) Yesterday's market turned active. Arrivals were still shipped from various ports along the Yangtze River. Production areas were seeking sales by transferring shipments to Shanghai because sales in Guangdong were stagnant. However, merchants in Guangdong preferred to directly arrange shipments from Hunan Province, complaining about cumbersome procedures and various inspections and difficulties. Yesterday, they also purchased 2,000 packages of Han rough rice in the Shanghai market, and the North Ocean Organic Red Mill was sold out. Shantou and Zhengzhou continued to arrange purchases, and the countryside and villages in this street also had smooth purchases, and the market turned active. The total daily sales were more than 6,000 packages of Gan rice, 561 packages of Xiang rice, 2,000 packages of Han silk, and 4,200 packages of Ningbo Jiaxing rice, totaling 12,300 packages. With the active trading, the price also jumped up by 5-6 fen to beyond a Jiao.

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources for each trading house were slightly scarce, with a total of more than 60 houses arriving, with a total of 12,4-500 dan of goods, of which there were more than 40 houses of thin rice. Although the sales market in this street was not weak, the appetite was mediocre. Trading houses such as Pingjin Qingyan only traded 4-5,000 packages of thin rice, so the thin rice market became stable and did not fluctuate. Thick Japonica rose by one jiao due to the scarcity of goods, and Du Yangjian was also tight, and Yinyuan was also close to a jiao.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were only a few ships arriving from various places downstream, only 26-7 houses. The sales of white japonica, the hoarding households and retail sales in the early market continued to move, but the market slackened in the afternoon, and the market price rose by another 1-2 jiao. The shop sales of thin rice were quite active, and the price was more than two jiao higher. Early rice followed the price increase of about a Jiao, and the warehouse absorption of Baiyuan was activated, and the price was increased by 2-3-4 fen. Yangdu and other sen rice were priced up by one jiao, and the Yinyuan price was also tightened by more than a Jiao. Changbang special white japonica was not open yesterday.

Special Feature: Production, Sales, and Manufacturing of Qihong Tea (Continued Part 2)

Qihong black tea is mainly sold abroad. Therefore, all boxed tea is transported to Shanghai and sold to foreign firms. Very little is sold in retail stores. The Qihong black tea price mentioned in this section refers specifically to the market price in Shanghai. According to the Shanghai Commodity Price Quarterly and Monthly published by the National Tariff Commission of the Ministry of Finance, the market price of Qihong is based on the wholesale price in Shanghai on the 15th of each month. Page 16

Spring and Autumn

Increased Soybean Sales

The miscellaneous grains market was closed the day before yesterday in celebration of Chairman Chiang, so trading in the market was lively yesterday. Soybean sales were driven by oil pressing factories and inland oil mills, and the number of transactions increased sharply. It is estimated that 123 carloads of Sipingjie soybeans, 4 carloads of Bengbu soybeans, 3 carloads of Zhengcheng soybeans, 500 packages of Pizhou soybeans, 1 carload of Zhuang soybeans, more than 1,000 packages of other Za soybeans, 400 packages of Chi soybeans, and more than 100 packages of Dingjiazhou soybeans were traded. Prices rose by six or seven points to one dime compared to last Saturday. In short, the Dalian soybean market had more gains than losses, and the exchange's standard prices were therefore strong. Most traders aimed to profit from arbitrage, so the amount of spot goods outside was reduced, and it was not easy to find small quantities in the market.

Sugar Market: 10,000+ Bags of Dutch White Arrived Yesterday

The sugar market trend was stable and attractive yesterday. The guild's price was 21.60 yuan for spot No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar and 6.22 yuan for transshipment goods. No. 9 Dutch red KD mark rose another 5 points to 16.10 yuan. Dongbai No. 489 and the local factory's cotton white sugar remained unchanged. The price board showed Guangbang offering more than 300 packages of Zhu Qing at 12 yuan, and Jianbang offering more than 200 packages of Diao Qing at 12.80 yuan. Chao Bang offered dozens of packages of Huanggang Qing. It was heard from Shantou yesterday that due to Chiang's return to Nanjing, people's hearts were at peace, and various business groups resumed operations, pushing production prices up another 2 dimes. Yesterday, 10,360 bags of Dutch coarse white sugar were imported by the Zhini Canada ship.

North-South Goods: Sichuan Fungus Continues to Rise; Southern Gorgon Nut Sales are Better, Hence Rebound

The price of Sichuan fungus on the price board was 115 yuan, and dozens of consecutive trades had been made, but the market became tight again yesterday, rising another 5 yuan to 120 yuan before continuing to open trades. At the same time, production prices in Hankou also rose by 3-4 yuan, with the higher end at 100 yuan to 98 yuan. It is said that the top-quality small-packaged "Air Mail" brand sells for 115 yuan, with subsequent reductions, and the trend feels quite strong.

Southern Gorgon nut: Recently, in addition to occasional purchases from the Hua Bang, there is also demand from the local inland market, so the selling price has increased again compared to before. High-quality goods sell for 52 yuan, while the market for pond gorgon nut remains flat, with screened Zhuang selling for 18-19 yuan, and ordinary ones for 16-17 yuan.

Silk and Tea: Many American Silk Dealers' Telegrams Arrived in Shanghai

The Yokohama silk market rebounded slightly yesterday, with standard silk futures falling by 7 to 10 yuan. New York, however, followed in Yokohama's footsteps the day before, and both exchange and easy-to-hold prices rose sharply. Japanese silk at 83 cents rose by 9 cents, and 75 uniformity rose by 1 dime. Shanghai silk and Guangdong silk each rose by 9 cents. Exchange standard silk for December rose by 5 cents, and for May rose by 4.5 cents. In Lyon, only Japanese silk rose by half a franc, while other silk products sold at the original price. Many telegrams from American silk dealers arrived yesterday, but due to the overly strong sentiment in Shanghai, the volume of transactions was not large. 78 uniformity white silk from factories had a tendency to rise above 780 yuan on the selling board. Domestic sales of "B" grade were generally offered at 760 yuan. Sichuan white silk from factories also had considerable sales yesterday, and the price was firm, no less than that of Jiangsu and Zhejiang white silk from factories. Yesterday, a total of 188 packages were traded.

Hardware: Double-Coated American Tinplate Rises Sharply

The tinplate market has recently seen a turnaround, likely because overseas telegrams are reporting rising prices, and local inventories are scarce. Due to fears of a large price increase next spring, efforts are being made to purchase stock, causing prices to rise continuously, especially for double-coated American tinplate, which has risen by as much as 6-7 yuan. Currently, double-coated (90 lbs) American tinplate is quoted at 44 yuan, Italian goods at 41 yuan, and German goods at 40 yuan. As for double-coated (100 lbs) American goods, they are quoted at 50 yuan, Italian goods at 44 yuan, and German goods at 42 yuan. In addition, there is no market for British and French goods due to a shortage of supply. It is said that yesterday's trading saw the sale of 600+ boxes, purchased by hoarders and manufacturers.

Snippets

— (Tai Xuan)

The year is coming to an end. The Republic of China calendar on the desk, for the 25th year, has been flipped to the last one or two pages, with a thickness of several inches. "Another year has easily passed, and the spring breeze has returned." The wonderful years have passed in the blink of an eye.

We don't need to be saddened by the spring flowers and autumn moons, and we don't need to lament the increase in age. Let us examine the work and life we have done in this year, whether we have increased the efficiency of our work, or whether we have increased the progress of our studies and knowledge. For the country in distress, have we had a proper understanding and made our best efforts to save it? If we have a reasonably satisfactory answer, then this year has not been wasted. At the same time, we must also examine our personal lives, whether we have increased bad habits and bad customs, and use "if you have them, correct them; if you don't have them, be on guard" to warn ourselves.

The twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China is about to pass, and the twenty-sixth year is coming up next. The desk calendars are being prepared to be replaced with new ones. At the beginning of the first page of the Republic of China's twenty-sixth year, we hope that our personal lives, group lives, and national lives will have a new atmosphere like the new year. However, thinking of the international environment and the country that is being invaded, it naturally requires our entire nation to make greater efforts!

Gentlemen in Dance Halls and Soldiers on the Battlefield

— Yi Yun

What they wear:

Gentlemen – New Western suits, spring leather shoes; all ordered from abroad.

Soldiers – Silk wadded vests, national cloth military uniforms; all donated by the rear.

What they eat:

Gentlemen – Champagne, famous cigarettes, spearmint, coffee.

Soldiers – Yellow sand, fine mud, northwest wind, snowflakes.

What they hear:

Gentlemen – Royal band, playing famous melodies for dancing.

Soldiers – Gunfire and cannon fire, mixed with the tragic cries of wounded soldiers.

What they see:

Gentlemen – Couples embracing and the charming smiles of graceful dancers.

Soldiers – Waves of soldiers charging and the brutal massacre by the enemy.

What they smell:

Gentlemen – The fragrance of sugar, wine, and the perfume of the dancers.

Soldiers – The smell of gunpowder, explosives, and the bloody odor of the wounded.

What they shout:

Gentlemen – Good sister, come on! Give me a sweet kiss!

Soldiers – Brothers, kill them! What are a few wounds to be afraid of!

Ah, the gentlemen in the dance halls are still so happy! In the bright lights and on the smooth dance floor, they tightly embrace and dance, never thinking of those soldiers charging desperately in the rain of bullets and on the thick, frozen ice!

Dear readers! After reading the above comparison, we close our eyes and think carefully about which is the true glory.

Chunzi

— Wei Jing

Miss Chunzi is a waitress at a certain coffee shop I recently met in the past two months. She is Chinese. Her original name was not Chunzi. Because she joined the coffee shop three months ago, the boss gave her that alias.

The reason I noticed Miss Chunzi was because her unmuted local accent suggested that she and I might be from the same hometown. After inquiring, I learned that her hometown was only thirty miles away from mine, and that she came from a family of scholars and poets.

She is twenty-five years old this year, but she always says she is twenty-two to strangers. Because of her small body, saying she is twenty-two is enough. It is said that she left home at the age of seventeen. At that time, she was studying in Shanghai on her own. Due to the temptation of love, she did not hesitate to fall out with her conservative family and was driven out by her strict father. Because her mother was a stepmother, her brother was a wastrel, and her two older sisters had been married for many years, her feelings for them were very weak, so she left home without any nostalgia.

Then, she married her lover. Only after marriage did she realize that he was so cruel that it was impossible to live with him, and it was extremely difficult to find a trace of pleasant air in the family. After sixteen months, she gave birth to a child, who died less than a month later. As a result, the couple's life became even more miserable, and they argued every day. Finally, in the nineteenth month after their marriage, they unconditionally dissolved the bonds of mutual pain in a lawyer's office.

At that time, her heart was filled with pain, loneliness, and pessimism occupied her entire life. She wanted to continue her studies to acquire considerable living skills, but she felt that she lacked both the spirit and the economy. So she joined a song and dance troupe, mingled in the film circle, and even worked in several dance halls. In between, she left Shanghai twice and went to Hankou, Qingdao, and other places to make a living. In Hankou, she even worked in a factory for a time. During the January 28th Incident, she also worked as a volunteer nurse and then made nursing her profession. However, time flew by quickly, and after five or six years, she still hadn't found a foothold. So, three months ago, she was forced by hunger and cold to temporarily seek a living in the coffee shop, waiting for a chance to develop.

Once, I asked her if she would eventually return to marriage as her final destination. She shook her head with a bitter smile. She said, "In these five or six years of drifting around, I don't know how many men I have seen, and I don't know how many men have pursued me. But one's life is just a mess, and marriage, although it can solve the problem of bread, the mental pain is very severe. I understand this clearly."

Last Sunday, when I went to that coffee shop, she told me that her stepmother had died and her father was calling her home. But she hadn't decided yet. Yesterday, when I went to that coffee shop again with a friend, her companion said that she had received another letter from her father, resigned, and returned to her hometown the night before last. So I prayed for her, blessing this homeless little crow, to return to the embrace of her family and restore her original happiness, and to heal the deep wounds she had suffered in the past seven or eight years. May the light shine on the path she is about to take.

Winter Sweet

— Qing Qu

In the past, Fan Shihou wrote a treatise on plum blossoms, counting nearly a hundred species, but many flowers had three names, and in reality, there were only half that number. Some flowers bloom early, even before the Beginning of Winter, but this is because of the warm climate in Luofu and Yu Ling. Therefore, the ancients had the saying, "The plum blossoms on the ridge bloom first in October." In places like Wuxia, West Lake, Kuaiji, and Siming, although there are many century-old trees with branches twisted in myriad ways, providing a cool shade all around, under which dozens of people can sit, scholars and hermits often bring wine to appreciate them, but it is not easy for them to bloom until the end of winter and the coming of spring.

As for wintersweet, although it has the name "plum," it is not actually a plum blossom because it blooms at the same time as plum blossoms and its fragrance is similar. Its color is like beeswax, so it is called "wintersweet." Some say that it always blooms in the twelfth lunar month, so it is also called "twelfth plum," but the explanation varies. According to the classification of the tree, it is a deciduous shrub with long oval leaves that grow in pairs, unlike true plum blossoms, and it is also a unique flower with horizontal and slender branches. There are three types of flowers: bell-shaped, lotus-shaped, and dog-English, with the bell-shaped being the most valuable. The petals are round, the color is yellow, and the shape is similar to white plum blossoms. Even when in full bloom, it often looks like it is only half open. If you cut off a branch and place it in a vase, the fragrance can fill the room and last for a month, so people often pair it with nandina and place it in a vase to celebrate the season, considering it an indispensable elegant item in winter.

Behind my house, there is a vacant pond, and all other plants and trees have been abandoned and almost completely desolate, but only this wintersweet remains. It was planted by my late father, and it has been almost a hundred years since then. Therefore, the old branches are intertwined horizontally and vertically, not just two or three, and the withered branches are as large as a strong man's arm, and cannot be grasped. In recent years, without pruning, it feels even more picturesque. In addition, in winter, it is as if spring is coming, and the branches are full of golden-yellow flowers, and the fragrance spreads everywhere. Compared to last year, the flowers are blooming earlier, which is truly a rare phenomenon. As the saying goes, "After the winter solstice, the third 'xu' day is 'la'," but it is not that time yet, so I record it, which is also enough to see the gradual changes in the microclimate.

Recording Orangutan Blood

— Zhang Huang

Orangutan blood is the highest grade of red pigment; because it is taken from live orangutans, its color is particularly vivid, and its price is naturally not cheap. The story of how people obtain orangutan blood is quite interesting.

Hunters set out with flasks of fine wine and all the necessary supplies, and wait on the roadside that orangutans usually pass by. When the orangutans are about to approach, they quickly open the flasks, pour the wine into several large bowls, and arrange them on the road. They vigorously fan the large fans, so that the aroma of the wine spreads everywhere. The hunters then retreat to a hidden place by the roadside and watch secretly. Orangutans always travel in groups, and although they have no clothes on their bodies, they like to wear wooden clogs, making a *ga-da, ga-da* sound when they walk, thinking that they are as majestic as humans! This is exactly the way to give people an opportunity.

Orangutans' love of wine seems to be innate, with no difference between young and old. If there is wine today, they will definitely not return home until they are drunk! They suddenly smell the aroma of wine, which hits their mark, and they all drag their feet forward. Sure enough, they see the bowls of green liquid on the road, and everyone can't help but cheer and shout. However, there are always some older ones who are suspicious of such an unearned reward. Perhaps the danger is not far away, and they have not forgotten the past events. They are about to raise their glasses, but suddenly withdraw their hands, as if a tragic illusion is reflected in front of their eyes. They then drive away the group of young orangutans, while they make chirping sounds, seemingly warning each other not to commit the same mistake. After lingering slightly in this way, the group eventually leaves together.

Not far away, many of them frequently turn their heads, then stop and hesitate, and finally the whole group returns quickly. After going back and forth three or four times, they really can't restrain the temptation of the fragrant aroma, and begin to take small sips to satisfy their cravings. Certainly, once they have started, how can they be willing to stop? So the wine in the bowls is emptied in a rush, until there is no drop left in the bowls, and they have all drunk so much that they have no strength left, and they fall drunk on the roadside in a chaotic mess!

The hunters then jump out at this time, each raising a white blade high, pretending to be menacing, as if they are about to end their lives. They have no way to escape, and can only make pleading sounds. One hunter first stabs an orangutan with a knife, takes a vessel to receive its blood, and points it to the other orangutans to see. They can then understand, and each points to the place on their body where blood can be taken and stabbed with a knife. They will also act out gestures to show the amount of blood they can each supply, so as not to lose their lives, and let you take it as you wish.

Isn't it? "Give me fine wine, and I will repay you with bloody blood." Is it cheap to eat? Can cravings not be restrained completely? We can only look at the source of this orangutan blood!

Swapped Nests of Luan and Phoenix

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 9: Vows of the Heart with a Cup of Water, Talks of Withered Love Under the Green Lamp; Agreement with Gold Rings, Reporting Longing with Red Beans

The mystery had not been solved, and the next morning, Youmei came again. Today she was wearing the white bamboo cloth uniform from school, and also carried a white cloth schoolbag, simply looking like she was going to school. She was also coming more often, and upon entering the gate, she shouted "Cousin," and went straight to the study. When Guoqi saw this, he was about to reach for his long gown on the coat rack, but Youmei stretched out both arms and stopped him, laughing: "Cousin, if you are like this, you are being too polite. I am someone who comes every day, like a member of the family, why bother with such formalities? Don't you see that I am wearing casual clothes when I come here, and I don't think of coming here as a guest." Guoqi said: "I don't treat Miss Li as a guest either. If I treated Miss Li as a guest, the accommodations in the house would be inadequate." Youmei seemed to feel that there were too many pleasantries, which was close to boring, so she put the schoolbag on the table, with a smile breaking out, and said: "I searched through the trunk, and all I found was this package, big and small. As for which are useful materials and which are waste, I don't know, please choose for yourself." Guoqi was very happy to hear her say that she had brought many historical materials about the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, and he forgot to avoid suspicion. He immediately rushed forward to pick up the manuscripts and looked at them carefully. In fact, there was no need to look closely, just looking at the color of the paper from afar was enough to be disappointed. It turned out that they were all eight-line letter papers of bright red or peach red, on which were written in regular script nothing more than some old clichés congratulating the New Year. Although the dates were all from the Xianfeng and Tongzhi years, they were just letters of greeting from minor officials of the Qing court to their superiors, and not a single word mentioned the fighting with the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom. Even if there were some words about pacifying the rebellious atmosphere, they were not historical materials. He looked at twenty or thirty pieces in a row, and they were all like this. Youmei did not say anything while he was looking at these documents. She stood quietly by his side, waving a fan in her hand. Although she was fanning herself to cool off, the wind from the fan was generally blowing towards Guoqi. Guoqi initially did not know this while he was looking at the letters. Later, he stopped momentarily and understood. However, although he was very grateful to her in his heart, he could not say it clearly, so he smiled at her and said: "There are too many things, I can't see clearly for a while." Youmei had forgotten herself and was still fanning the fan herself, also fanning Guoqi, and said: "It doesn't matter. No one in my family has ever touched these documents, so just leave them here with you. Whenever you are done looking at them, return them to me. These things are not my personal property. If they were my personal property, I would give them to my brother." (to be continued)

Special Feature

Year-End Scenes

— Xia Fei

—A cross-section of Nanjing Road

The metropolis's artery, stretching toward the racetrack, throbs intensely; the tense crowds flow like blood in the veins. The neon lights on the billboards weave a tapestry of red and green in the air, while the spires of the four major department stores stand quietly in the northwest wind. The flags of the winter sales are densely hung in front of the shops on both sides, and the radio broadcasts New Year's Eve marches, making everyone realize that a long year has quietly crept past behind their anxious lives.

Nanjing Road, the commercial hub of this "Paris of the East," is always so prosperous, so beautiful. Every day, from early morning to late at night, whether it is winter or summer, it never conceals its lively and bustling appearance. The pedestrians, like a swarm of ants, and the vehicles, like a swarm of ants, move from east to west and from west to east. The red and green traffic lights change colors busily, never stopping or becoming quiet for a single moment.

Starting from the Bund, the Sassoon House towers over the rolling Huangpu River. At the intersection of Jiangxi Road, several blood-sucking tubes of the great powers are erected there, with their mouths aimed directly at the city's blood vessels, at every pore of the Chinese people, absorbing large amounts of blood. This economic aggression is no less powerful than artillery.

From the Bowling Green to the New World, that is the most intense scene on Nanjing Road. Here, the large glass windows of the shops display various rare and beautiful goods. There are large silk and satin shops, large fur shops for clothing, large food companies and large tonic shops for food, large furniture companies and large department stores for use; in short, there are all kinds of modern things here. As long as you have enough legal tender in your pocket, then you can get anything you want. If your pocket is "empty," I think it is better to walk away quickly, so as not to get itchy eyes.

In every corner, shadows are wriggling, all of them busy, as if they are doing some secret deals. Some shops, companies, amusement parks, dance halls, and food stores are rushing to decorate for the New Year. In front of several southern goods stores, many dazzling electric lights have been installed, and the customers are indeed attracted to them quite lively. They all come out of the store with bundles of paper packages in their arms, with a satisfied smile on their faces.

In the section near the Rising Sun Building, a row of "goddesses" selling their chastity stand on the sidewalks. For the sake of survival, they cannot enjoy the leisure and comfort of New Year's Eve like ordinary people. As usual, they have to stand in the cold northwest wind on the streets late at night, waiting for someone to come and satisfy their lives, and at the same time, they are willing to let him satisfy his sexual desire once; in this way, both parties are satisfied under the terms of a buying and selling transaction.

In the dead of night, when the loud bells of the Jianghai Customs Station drift into every corner of the city, Nanjing Road, that sinful, prosperous, commercial hub, also lies quietly there like a hibernating giant snake. But it will still be just as active tomorrow morning.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

The Tragic Decline of the Real Estate Industry

— Zhou Ge

For someone who lives on a salary, his expenses can be said to be one-third, or even one-half, spent on the issue of "housing." The so-called "land is as valuable as gold" is indeed true in Shanghai!

In recent years, the speculative business of real estate can be said to have entered a state of recession, just like other sectors of the economy. Recently, the Real Estate Industry Association submitted a petition to the Shanghai Municipal Government, detailing the tragic decline in land prices and requesting that the Land Bureau reassess land prices and reduce taxes. The petition stated, "In recent years, due to the decline in commerce and the exhaustion of the market in Shanghai, the fall in land prices has been precipitous. Therefore, the real estate industry is the one that suffers the most among commercial sectors. The trend is such that there are often cases of people being bankrupted..." We cannot deny that this tragic situation of falling land prices, which has led to the bankruptcy of real estate businesses, is a true reflection of the facts. In today's increasingly deepening national crisis, this phenomenon is a common one, not surprising!

If those who have land are "suffering" so much, and say that they are the ones who suffer the most, then those who do not have land, especially the ordinary wage earners, their "suffering" is certainly a thousand times greater! Since the January 28th Incident, especially in the past year or two, the general second landlords of Shanghai's lane houses, some of whom used to rely on renting out a building to people and could even make a living, now seem like a golden dream of the past. Second landlords are now full of complaints, and the disputes between tenants (mostly second landlords) and landlords can be said to rise and fall one after another, without end. Although we still cannot see the panic of the second landlords in the more central areas, in areas secondary to the central area, on every lane entrance, square red paper "For Rent" signs, like plasters, are plastered all over the walls. And a closer look at the text of the "For Rent" signs seems to be very "progressive," mostly rich in artistic "allure," as if the "literaryization" of advertising can be smelled in the "For Rent" signs. If the second landlords are still like this, the "third landlords" are certainly "worse than the second"!

The suffering of real estate businesses is indeed a fact, and the miserable situation of tenants is even more undeniable. In today's deepening national crisis, we really cannot point out a path we should take!

Thoughts Inspired by the "Support Suiyuan Concert"

— Yin Fei

"All art is propaganda." We hear this sentence often. This sentence is absolutely correct.

Some people regard "art" as something unattainable; others regard art as something to cultivate emotions and please the mind. For example, in the film industry, there are so-called "soft school" advocates who believe that movies should only be used as "ice cream for the eyes and a sofa chair for the soul."

But what exactly is "art"? The two words "art" do indeed seem sacred and unattainable. Even if it is unattainable, it cannot but be related to the human world. Once it is related to the human world, objectively, it cannot but have an effect. Moreover, there is also the subjectivity of the "artist" in the middle, and the "artist" is the same as ordinary people, needing to eat and sleep and unable to walk in the air.

After the Suiyuan Incident occurred, regarding the assistance to the soldiers defending the front lines, we are not exaggerating when we say that it can be described as a "national uprising." If we further investigate the occupations and ages of the donors in this "national uprising," we would be even more moved to tears. However, in this regard, how much effort has the art world—let's expand the scope a bit and call it the cultural world—put in? Speaking of which, the cultural world should logically be the guide of the people.

I don't know how it is in other places, but in Shanghai, from what I have seen, people in the art world are lagging behind other people. Not only have they failed to take the lead, but, ridiculously, they are being led by the enthusiasm of the people.

Since the Suiyuan Incident, up to now, let's calculate and see if there have been any exhibitions or other gatherings to promote national self-defense? Sadly, there have been a few, such as the joint broadcasts by several singing groups specializing in broadcasting on the radio, and some piecemeal photography exhibitions with proceeds going to support Suiyuan, and so on. Being able to find ways to raise some money within one's "own position" to help the soldiers defending the territory is naturally commendable. However, is this enough to fulfill one's responsibility, friends engaged in art?

Based on the understanding that "all art is propaganda," in addition to material assistance, we should also have more spiritual assistance. Spiritual assistance is not only directly given to the soldiers defending the front lines, but more importantly, it also lies in how to arouse the passionate patriotic emotions of the people in the rear and how to guide the people to a unified path of resistance. The war of national self-defense can only have a chance of victory if the entire nation is mobilized.

Recently, there was a support Suiyuan concert held by the music community in Shanghai. This is naturally a good thing. Looking at the program list, there were songs such as "The Chinese Nation Will Not Perish," "Song of the Goddess of Liberty," "Who Says We Are Too Young," and "The Flag is Waving" (but also "Three Rose Wishes," etc.). In terms of content, it can be said that the music community has fulfilled its responsibilities. Using skills within one's "own position" to sell tickets to support Suiyuan is the duty of a citizen. And for people in the art world to contribute to the nation and society with their duties is also their duty within their "own position." If one uses decadent music to enchant the audience and takes the opportunity to exchange it for some money to donate to the soldiers defending the front lines, then in terms of the duty of a citizen, it can naturally be considered fulfilled, but in terms of the duty of one's position, he is a sinner! This sin cannot be offset by fulfilling the duty of a citizen. The reason is that...

Page 18

...fulfilling the duty of a citizen is originally one's duty, but using decadent music to numb the people is a sin!

And now, there seem to be quite a few who have forgotten the "duty of one's position" for the sake of the "duty of a citizen"!

The Shanghai music community's support Suiyuan concert naturally takes both into consideration, but for the sake of fulfilling the duty of one's position, I hope that it can be done more deeply and more universally. At times, the duty of one's position is more important than the duty of a citizen.

Of course, this is not only hoping that the music community will do this, but even more so, it is not only hoping that the music community in Shanghai will do this.

If a cultural worker cannot do more than the average citizen in patriotism, then he is ashamed of the two words "culture"!

Willow

— Liao Chuxiu

Among plants, I love willows the most. The "Flower Mirror" divides willows into two types. It says about the willow: "The willow is also called the official willow, or the weeping willow. Its nature is soft and brittle. It grows in the north, with many long and soft branches, and green and long leaves. In early spring, it produces catkins, thick as tendons, about an inch long, with yellow flowers. The scales fall off the catkins, very fine and scattered, gradually growing leaves. By late spring, the leaves are fully grown, with small seeds inside, like millet grains, flat, small and black, with white fluff like velvet, commonly known as willow catkins, which fly in the wind. They cause moths in wool clothing and turn into duckweed in ponds. This is the official willow. If the leaves form shade, with long branches several feet or even over ten feet long, swaying downwards, this is the weeping willow. Although it has no fragrance, it sways in the breeze and is often the place where orioles sing and cicadas rest. People take it to please their ears and eyes, and it is a necessary tree in gardens." It says about the poplar: "There are two types of poplar. The white poplar has white hair when its buds are sprouting, and when fully unfolded, its leaves are like pear leaves, long and thick, light green on the surface and white on the back, with long stems that face each other in pairs. When the wind blows, they rustle. People often plant them in cemeteries. They can grow over ten feet tall. There is also the green poplar tree, which is smaller than the white poplar, with leaves that resemble apricot leaves but are slightly longer and larger, and are green in color. Its trunk is also straight. Generally, willow branches are long and brittle, with narrow and long leaves, while poplar branches are short, with round and wide leaves. Willows thrive in water, while poplars thrive in drought. The two trees are not the same, so how can one assume they are the same tree simply because they are mentioned together?"

Here, the two types of willows and poplars are distinguished very clearly. However, the one I love is the "weeping willow" with "leaves forming shade, long branches several feet or even over ten feet long, swaying downwards." But I am, after all, an "ordinary person," and I do not believe the saying that "willow catkins turn into duckweed in ponds," and I call "weeping willows" willows and poplars without distinction.

Liu Tingzhi's "Gongzi Xing" says: "Pitiful willow, heart-breaking tree." When I read this, I had a sense of enlightenment, because the three words "heart-breaking tree" are really a good posthumous name for the willow, a name that can truly capture the soul of the willow. I have not read many books, and I don't know if there are people who regard willows as plants of joy. But I have certainly never seen them.

The "Shishuo Xinyu" says: "When Duke Huan went north to conquer, he passed through Jincheng and saw that the willows planted when he was the Prince of Langya were already ten spans around. He sighed and said, 'Even the trees are like this, how can people bear it?' He grasped the branches and wept." Also, "Gu Yue and Jianwen were the same age, but his hair turned white early. Jianwen said, 'Why did you turn white first?' He replied, 'My figure is like a reed willow, falling at the sight of autumn, while the quality of pine and cypress becomes more luxuriant after frost.'" Therefore, Duke Xuanwu of Huan already had a sense of lateness because the willows were already ten spans around, so he knew that among plants, the willow is also one that "falls early." Compared to pine and cypress, how could he not feel sorrow?

In ancient times, people often broke off willow branches as gifts, so Tang Xianzu's "The Purple Hairpin" in the "Folding Willow at Yangguan" says: "Although Scholar Li is bravely departing today, it is difficult to teach this concubine not to be sad. The Baling Bridge is ahead. This concubine will fold a willow branch before the wine and express my thoughts of Yangguan." Then there is a branch of mistletoe: "Fearing to play the Yangguan tune, the Wei River feels cold, all the peach leaves of Jianggan crossing the waves, the green grass of Tingzhou sticking to the clouds. This willow color of the river bridge welcomes the wind, (folding the willow) Willow! Your slender waist makes a cord to tie people, how laughable that your own catkins are hard to hold." The classic of folding willow at Yangguan naturally comes from Wang Wei's poem: "Weicheng morning rain moistened the light dust, the guesthouse is green, the willow color is new; I urge you to drink one more cup of wine, going west out of Yangguan, there are no old friends." It is said that at that time, the willow trees beside the official road often had their long branches broken off, leaving only bare large branches.

Jiang Yaozhang of the Southern Song Dynasty was famous for his poems, but his prefaces to the poems were actually ten thousand times better than his poems: "Many willows are planted inside Hefei City. When the autumn wind rises in the evening, they rustle." These few words have already depicted the scene of a desolate city in late autumn, yet he only described the willows.

There are really too many works about willows and poplars from ancient times to the present. But what I like the most is Yang Fengbao's "Autumn Willows of West Lake." Because he entrusted a deep and remote feeling, unlike Wang Xincheng's four regulated verses on "Autumn Willows," which tasted like chewing wax. Now I will copy two poems here as the ending of my short essay.

"The misty rain makes the lake and mountains look like the sad eyebrows of a beauty, and the brocade sails send you far away to Yangzhou; I regret that I do not have Chen Fan's spring breeze brush to paint the ink painting of the Southern Dynasty."

"The hall of ten thousand acres is deep and the moon is dark, the singing and dancing in the new pond are unbearable, where are the flying catkins of the Xie family returning to? Only the tender yellow remains to illuminate the night millstone." These two poems really have a feeling of national demise, so the rustling willows, what difference is there from the millet and wheat of Shuli?

Jiang Bin Chu's "Three Smiles"

New Sound (1380) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening: "Sudden Change"

The sky is light, the wind is clear, and the air is refreshing. Several lines of new geese pass through the air. The busy attendant, Gao Lishi, is sweeping and cleaning in the Royal Garden with great effort. The autumn scenery in the inner garden is endless, with lotus flowers remaining everywhere in the ponds. After a while, it is reported that Emperor Ming has arrived, supported by his favorite concubine, Yang Guifei. Countless osmanthus flowers are fragrant in the wind, and sometimes parrots call to each other. The imperial banquet is arranged on the flower pavilion, and the tables are filled with delicacies from the sea and mountains. Slender jade hands hold golden pots. The emperor beats the rhythm, the concubine sings, and the dance of the rainbow skirt is unparalleled in the world. Taizhen kneels and presents three cups of wine, and the Emperor joyfully holds and supports her hand. Yang Guifei falls drunk on the couch, a picture of a begonia sleeping in spring. Seeing her drunken and charming appearance, he is even more enchanted. Who would have known that joy was not over before sorrow arrived? It is said that An Lushan launched a rebellion and wielded weapons, directly approaching the capital city. What to do? The Tang Dynasty had enjoyed peace for a long time, and the civil and military officials were unable to resist the enemy. They quickly ordered the Six Armies to protect the emperor. Suddenly, carriages and horses rushed on their long journey, temporarily escaping the smoke of war to fortunate themselves in Shu. Pitifully, the weak and beautiful woman, like a flower, perishes and her fragrance vanishes in a piece of silk, bestowed death at Mawei Slope in a moment.

The Shanghai Harmonica Society at 252 Wenmiao Road, Ximen, this city. Since the first session of slightly charging free members, the number of applicants has been extremely enthusiastic. Later applicants have mostly felt disappointed due to the quota being full, and have requested that more classes be opened. This shows that the society is well-managed. Now, in response to the requests of all sectors, the society is specifically seeking new free male and female comrades for the second session, and has established branches at Shanggong Middle School at 186 Whiteker Road (behind the International Hotel) and the South Station Fellow Club. Tuition and fees are waived, and there are advanced classes, beginner autumn classes, harmonica teams, and women's classes. Those interested in studying can quickly register. Registration is limited to the number of places available. Classes start on the 3rd and 4th of this month.

Movies

Behind-the-Scenes at Lianhua Studio

Li Lili is skilled in rhetoric. Every time she talks and laughs in a gathering, the whole room is filled with spring, as if there is a kind of heat that attracts people to get close to her. Whenever Fei Mu sees Lili, he welcomes her and says: "Spring has arrived in the world."

All colleagues in the factory who have a new haircut must greet everyone they meet. Otherwise, they will be beaten three times. It is not known when or by whom this custom originated. One day, after Yin Xiucen had his haircut, he met a large crowd as usual. Suddenly, he heard a whistle and was slapped on his fat head. At the same time, he heard the curse: "Three slaps for a haircut, no syphilis, no sores."

In "Daughter of the General," Han Langan plays a soldier who, in order to release a serious criminal, is demoted to a groom. He feeds and washes the horses in the stable, singing war songs. He deliberately acts shyly, exposing several bare "oily ribs." The staff at the scene could not help but cover their mouths and laugh.

In "Spring Arrives in the World," Han Langan and Shang Guanwu play butchers who tie up pigs to be slaughtered. But Han is timid as a mouse, assisting from the side, lowering his eyebrows and closing his eyes, not daring to look directly. Shang, on the other hand, holds a knife and stabs directly. As a result, Han is appropriately covered in pig blood, blurring his facial features.

Chen Yanyan loves old music songs the most. Her residence next to the Lianhua factory often emits clear and graceful singing, Yanyan, Yangko, etc.

Mei Xishan is good at writing articles and often writes drafts for the Lianhua Factory Newspaper. Her writing is clear and smooth, and her arguments are superb.

In "Spring Arrives in the World," there is a bamboo ware cradle shop and a stone tablet engraving shop next to each other, showing the course of life. From cradle to grave, the journey is very short. Chen Yanyan plays the maid Xiaohong in the play, struggling reluctantly under the oppression of violence, spending her days in tears.

Grand Light Screens "The Charge of the Light Brigade"

Costing Two Million, Sending Seven Thousand People

Warner Bros.' war film "The Charge of the Light Brigade," which has been rumored for a long time, will be publicly screened at the Grand Light Theater starting today. During this year, we have seen American war films such as "Gold Diggers of 1935," "The Story of Louis Pasteur," "The Life of Emile Zola," and so on... But compared to this "The Charge of the Light Brigade," they are all "dwarfed by comparison." In short, this film has achieved amazing achievements in terms of performance. The cruelty makes people's hair stand on end, the tension makes people's blood boil, the eroticism makes people's souls melt away, and the sadness makes people's tears fall and their hearts ache. Moreover, at this time of national crisis, watching the six hundred martyrs on the silver screen charging towards the enemy's cannons, you cannot help but feel excited, you cannot help but applaud. As for the acting skills of the protagonist, Errol Flynn, they are also above the great star Colman. It is also heard that Grand Light, in order to particularly please the audience, will simultaneously screen the Technicolor cartoon "The Two Little Bears."

Special Program of the Drama Friendship Society: Morning of Drama and Dance

The Drama Friendship Society is an organization for drama practitioners to connect and foster relationships. Since its establishment, its work has been very intense. It regularly holds gatherings every week. The society has now scheduled a special gathering at 10:00 AM on New Year's Eve this year at the Carlton Theater, inviting Wu Xiaobang, the only artistic dancer in China, to perform stage dance. Dance art is still in its infancy in China, and this move is worthy of our attention. It is now learned that the society has printed invitations and distributed them to drama and film circles, as well as groups and individuals who love drama art, so that they can enjoy the event together. Drama groups or newspapers that have not received this invitation can send a representative to the society at 3 Xirong Villa, Huanlong Road to collect it, or call 72069 to inquire. It is said that there are not many tickets left, so those who want to collect them should do so early, lest they miss the opportunity.
